# 3.21 Remote Interference Management

## 3.21.0-3 Remote Interference Management Document Owner Deputy Feifeng Qin (ID: 11160798)

## 3.21.1 DL scheduling

### 3.21.1.0-1 DL scheduling RIM framework activation and configuration (ID: 11160807)

**3.21.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11160837`)

DL scheduling
11160837:
DL scheduling
When RIM feature flag NRBTS/NRCell-actNrRim is NOT configured 0-"disable" ,

- NR cell shall enter RI state 0 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9319\_replaced([11161316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktTTrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- Once actNrRim is configured to 3-"framework-0"[CB009823-A] or 4-"framework-1"[End CB009823-A], gNB-DU shall determine configuration for the first RIM RS transmission period

o Determine RIM RS transmission periodicity [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of the letters "P" and "c" in a stylized font. The letters are rendered in a gradient of colors, with shades of orange, yellow, blue, and purple. The background is white, and the image is framed by a thick black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11078.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12626\_replaced([11117421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

o Determine resource configuration

 configuration for RIM RS type 1 generation (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12629\_replaced([11117907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 frequency domain configuration for RIM RS transmission  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13076\_replaced([11117993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 time domain allocation for RIM RS transmission  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13070\_replaced([11117417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 sequence domain configuration for RIM RS transmission (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12686\_replaced([11118096](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- upon the online reconfigure RIM profile during current period, gNB-DU shall update the configuration calculated as above for next RIM RS transmission period.

- At the end of each RIM RS transmission period (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13455\_replaced([11117569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  ,  gNB-DU shall update the configuration calculated as above for next RIM RS transmission period

- At the beginning of each RIM RS transmission period (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13455\_replaced([11117569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , gNB-DU shall implement the configuration calculated as above for this RIM RS transmission period

-     If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true,

 At the end of a pooling period, 5G-L2-PS shall reserve in pooling mechanism the number of cell PRBs to transmit RIM-RS in next pooling period(from the start of 2nd SFN in next pooling period to the end of first SFN in the pooling period after next pooling period), based on the calculated RIM-RS resource configurations above. If RIM-RS does not need to be transmitted in the pooling period, then number of cell PRBs to transmit RIM-RS in next pooling period is 0. Note: 10MHz cell does not support RIM-RS and thus number of cell PRBs to transmit RIM-RS in next pooling period is always 0.

 In case next pooling period(for the time between the start of 2nd SFN in next pooling period and the end of first SFN in the pooling period after next pooling period) in pooling mechanism overlaps with the last part of current RIM-RS period and the first part of next RIM-RS transmission period,

If new RIM-RS resource configuration has been calculated for next RIM-RS transmission period, then 5G-L2-PS shall always reserve in pooling mechanism the max number of cell PRBs between current RIM-RS resource configuration and new calculated RIM-RS resource configuration, based on whether RIM-RS needs to be transmitted or not in next pooling period(which overlaps last part of current RIM-RS transmission period and first part of next RIM-RS transmission period). Note: It is a corner case and could happen that RIM-RS transmission is at the end of a RIM-RS period and also at beginning of next RIM-RS transmission period, with very specific online reconfiguration in current RIM-RS period.

 If new RIM-RS resource configuration has not been calculated for next RIM-RS transmission period, then 5G-L2-PS shall reserve in pooling mechanism the number of cell PRBs for RIM-RS transmission, only based on current RIM-RS resource configuration and whether RIM-RS needs to be transmitted in current RIM-RS transmission period.

---

### 3.21.1.0-2 DL scheduling Request RIM RS type 1/2 transmission (ID: 11160843)

**3.21.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13476722`)

DL scheduling
13476722:
DL scheduling
gNB-DU shall trigger sending own RIM RS type 1 under following condition
- if *NRBTS/NRCELL-actNrRim = 3 (framework-0), and*
{ if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger= 1*
 or  ( if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger= 2 && RIstate=2  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))))*
 [CB015735-A]or NRRIM\_PROFILE-actRsContinuousDetect = True[End CB015735-A]
}
- if *NRBTS/NRCELL-actNrRim = 4 (framework-1), and*
{ if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger= (1 or 3)*
 or  ( if RIstate=2  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))))
[CB015735-A]or NRRIM\_PROFILE-actRsContinuousDetect = True[End CB015735-A]
} 
 
gNB-DU shall trigger sending own RIM RS type 2 under following condition
if *NRBTS/NRCELL-actNrRim = 4 (framework-1), and*
{ if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger= (1 or 4)*
 or  ( if RIstate=2b  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))))
} 
gNB-DU shall request PRB range resource (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13075\_replaced([11118073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on the slot (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12685\_replaced([11117748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the primary subcell where the RIM-RS repetition shall be sent.
gNB-DU shall determine the sequence configuration for RIM-RS type1 based on the "Enough" or "NotEnough" indication (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24844\_replaced([11162999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at the beginning of the repetition window (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12684\_replaced([11117616](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 
If the resource was available, gNB-DU shall request sending own RIM RS type 1 per repetition opportunity containing following resource allocation:
- Pattern ID from beam set #1 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1933\_replaced([11111686](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpPTD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- The indications of slot , frame and SFN where RIM-RS type1 shall be sent (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12685\_replaced([11117748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
- Frequency range
 > if actNrRim=3-"framework-0", the frequency range is indicated by start PRB index (k1, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12631\_replaced([11117996](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAICPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PRB number (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13075\_replaced([11118073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
 > if actNrRim=4-"framework-1", the frequency range is indicated by start PRB index (rimRsPrbOffset, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13075\_replaced([11118073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ), sub-carrier offset (RimRsSubCarrierOffset, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13075\_replaced([11118073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PRB number  see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13075\_replaced([11118073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
- power level setting  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12777\_replaced([11118655](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqEZefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
 
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true,
          RIM-RS of newly setup cells or newly activated RIM-RS framework-0 cells (with online reconfigure NRCELL/actNRRim=3) or newly activated RIM-RS framework-1 cells (with online reconfigure NRCELL/actNrRim=4) during a pooling period shall not be transmitted until receiving allocation from pooling mechanism for the pooling period after next pooling period. Because PRBs of RIM-RS transmissions may not be reserved properly in pooling mechanism, and the L1 Pool capacity may be exceeded.
          RIM-RS can be transmitted in case allocated PRBs from pooling mechanism are enough.
          If (actBeamforming is false and dlMiMoMode is "ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_4x4 or OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_4x4" (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) or (dlSubcellType of Primary Subcell is "C2"),
     RIM-RS can be transmit when allocated cell PRBs to the cell >= required cell PRBs for RIM-RS transmission.
          Else If (actBeamforming is true and dlSubcellType of Primary Subcell is "C4") 
  RIM-RS can be transmit when allocated cell PRBs to the cell >= required cell PRBs for RIM-RS transmission/2.
          Else
  RIM-RS is not transmitted.
          End If
          Note: dlSubcellType which is in dlSubcellList, actBeamforming and dlMimoMode are from PsCell\_CellSetupReq message (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
 
          Successfully allocated cell PRBs from pooling mechanism should be enough for RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period, since allocation of DL minimum PRBs for a cell has considered the requested PRBs for RIM-RS transmission(5G\_UP\_ALG\_13342\_replaced([11212500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). PRBs for RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period shall <=  previous reserved RIM-RS PRBs in pooling mechanism for the pooling period, since the cell may not be a ZAB cell.
          If the pooling period (from the start of 2nd SFN in current pooling period until the end of first SFN in next pooling period) overlaps with the last part of current RIM-RS transmission period and the first part of next RIM-RS transmission period, L2PS can only transmit RIM-RS in the first part of next RIM-RS transmission period if required PRBs for RIM-RS transmission <= previous reserved number of cell PRBs in pooling mechanism for the pooling period (from the start of 2nd SFN in current pooling period until the end of first SFN in next pooling period), see following figure for details.
          [image-5][image\_desc]The image displays a timeline illustrating the resource allocation for RIM-RS transmission periods and pooling periods. The timeline is divided into several colored segments representing different periods.
At the top, a horizontal bar shows:
- A segment labeled "Current RIM-RS transmission period" in yellow.
- A segment labeled "Next RIM-RS transmission period" in blue.
- Shorter segments at the beginning and end, indicated by "...".
Below this, another horizontal bar shows:
- A segment labeled "Previous pooling period" in red.
- A segment labeled "Current pooling period" in purple.
- A segment labeled "Next pooling period" in red.
There are vertical arrows and numbers indicating specific points in time:
- Arrow labeled "2" points to the boundary between "Current RIM-RS transmission period" and "Next RIM-RS transmission period".
- Arrows labeled "1", "3", and "4" point to specific locations within the pooling periods.
Below the timeline, there are four numbered steps and a conditional statement explaining the process:
**STEP 1.** At the end of previous pooling period, L2PS shall reserve in pooling mechanism the prbDemandRim for current pooling period, only based on RIM-RS resource configuration for current RIM-RS transmission period. Because RIM-RS resource configuration for next RIM-RS transmission period is calculated in STEP2, after STEP1.
**STEP 2.** Calculate RIM-RS resource configuration for next RIM-RS transmission period. Note: L2PS shall calculate RIM-RS resource configuration for next RIM-RS transmission period at the end of current RIM-RS transmission period.
**STEP 3.** Reserved PRBs for RIM-RS in pooling mechanism in STEP1 will be applied from 2nd SFN of current pooling period.
**STEP 4.** Reserved PRBs for RIM-RS in pooling mechanism in STEP1 will be applied until the end of 1st SFN of next pooling period.
**Conditional Statement:** If RIM-RS transmission in next RIM-RS transmission period is required in current pooling period (until 1st SFN in next pooling period in STEP4), and if required PRBs for RIM-RS transmission <= previous reserved prbDemandRim in STEP1 for current pooling period, then the RIM-RS is transmitted.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11082.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]
        
           A PM counter will record the discarded RIM-RS transmission in DL.
 
End If

### 3.21.1.0-3 DL scheduling RIM DL Mitigation (ID: 11160930)

**3.21.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11160935`)

DL scheduling
Overview

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12584463`)

DL scheduling
This chapter covers the following aspects of RIM DL mitigation:

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29880\_replaced([11160944](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3bPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'RIM DL mitigation triggers': This section describes the conditions that must be met to initiate any RIM DL mitigation.
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29881\_replaced([11161050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'RIM DL mitigated slots': This section determines the specific slots that will be affected by RIM DL mitigation.
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29882\_replaced([11161102](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'RIM DL muting' and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29883\_replaced([11161152](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSsk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'RIM DL power reduction': These sections detail the two available RIM DL mitigation methods. Each section outlines the additional conditions that must be met to apply the appropriate RIM DL mitigation method.
* [CB014157-A]  'RIM Pilot based DL muting' ([12562993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Z_XD0CrxEfCNjfqfyUlvmw)) : This section describes the conditions that must be met to apply the RIM pilot based DL muting. [End CB014157-A]

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11160944`)

DL scheduling
RIM DL mitigation triggers

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11160950`)

DL scheduling
Evaluation of RIM DL mitigation

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11160956`)

DL scheduling
If any of the following conditions is met:

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13208\_replaced([11163466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine DL mitigation on RIM-RS detection' or
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25962\_replaced([11163496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Manually triggered DL mitigation' or
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25980\_replaced([11163514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine DL mitigation based on RI detection'
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25961\_replaced([11163530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine DL mitigation based on mixed RIM-RS and RI detection'

Then this evaluation results with true.

Otherwise, results with false.

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11160959`)

DL scheduling
General

**3.21.1.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11160972`)

DL scheduling

**3.21.1.0-3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11160978`)

DL scheduling
Manually triggered DL mitigation

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11160988`)

DL scheduling
Note: since CB012719-A, this requirement is no longer maintained, as it is splitted into:

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29892\_replaced([11161067](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL mitigated slots for manually triggered DL muting'
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29900\_replaced([11161131](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Execute RIM DL muting'

[Before CB012719-A]

[Before CB013350-A]

If NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is NOT "0:disabled", gNB-DU shall determine if to mute special slot BIx y  and its last preceding DL slot (DL14 )  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger

[CB013350-A]

If all trigger conditions described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25962\_replaced([11163496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Manually triggered DL mitigation' are fulfilled, L2PS shall determine muted slots as described below:

[End CB013350-A]

* if rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "1:special slot muting"

> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following condtiions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true,

* K2 needs to be adjusted dynamcially as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PDCCH on special slot BIx y  shall be muted.
* else if rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "2:DL+special slots muting",

> PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be muted
>
> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following condtiions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true,

* K2 needs to be adjusted dynamcially as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PDCCH on special slot BIx y  shall be muted.
* else if rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "3:2DL+special slots muting",

> PDSCH in the last preceding 2 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be muted
>
> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following condtiions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true,

* K2 needs to be adjusted dynamcially as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PDCCH on special slot BIx y  shall be muted.

[Before CB013350-A]

gNB-DU shall stop UE traffic scheduling except msg2 and msg4 scheduling in those muted slots (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13518\_replaced([11173699](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuV1cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB013350-A]

In muted slots L2PS shall not schedule UE dedicated PDSCH transmission according to limitations described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13704\_replaced([11174307](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuat9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'DL Scheduling restrictions under Remote Interference Mitigation'.

[End CB013350-A]

The DL slot ( DL14 ) or the special slot BIx y where exists DL symbols used for RIM RS transmission (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13072\_replaced([11117793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall NOT be muted.

[End CB012719-A]

**3.21.1.0-3.0-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11161006`)

DL scheduling
Note: since CB012719-A, this requirement is no longer maintained, as it is splitted into:

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29894\_replaced([11161077](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL mitigated slots for RIM-RS based DL muting'

[Before CB012719-A]

[Before CB013350-A]

If NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "0:disabled" and NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim = (3 (framework-0) or “4:framework-1”), gNB-DU shall determine if to mute special slot BIx y  and its last preceding DL slot (DL14 )  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on maxRSSymbolDistance (see in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13204\_replaced([11163050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as below

[CB013350-A]

If all trigger conditions described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13208\_replaced([11163466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine DL mitigation on RIM-RS detection' are fulfilled, L2PS shall determine muted slots as described below:

[End CB013350-A]

* if maxRSSymbolDistance is not higher than x of BIx y ,

> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following conditions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true,

* K2 needs to be adjusted dynamcially as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PDCCH on special slot BIx y  shall be muted.
* else if maxRSSymbolDistance is not higher than 14+x (see x in BIx y)

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true,

* K2 needs to be adjusted dynamcially as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PDCCH on special slot BIx y  shall be muted.

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  ("1:DL+special slots muting" or "2:2DL+special slots muting"),
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be muted
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "0:special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

* else if maxRSSymbolDistance is higher than 14+x (see x in BIx y),

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true,

* K2 needs to be adjusted dynamcially as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PDCCH on special slot BIx y  shall be muted.

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "2:2DL+special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding 2 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be muted
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "1:DL+special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be muted
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "0:special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

* else, no slot of PDSCH shall be muted

[Before CB013350-A]

gNB-DU shall stop UE traffic scheduling except msg2 and msg4 scheduling in those muted slots (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13518\_replaced([11173699](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuV1cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB013350-A]

> >

>

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true,

* K2 needs to be adjusted dynamcially as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PDCCH on special slot BIx y  shall be muted.

>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be muted
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >

>

> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding 2 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be muted
> >

> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "1:DL+special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be muted
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be muted if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "0:special slots muting",
>

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11161050`)

DL scheduling
RIM DL mitigated slots

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11161055`)

DL scheduling
Determine RIM DL mitigated slots

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13432343`)

DL scheduling
L2PS shall determine RIM DL mitigated slots in the following way:

* [Before CB015505-A] If 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25962\_replaced([11163496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Manually triggered DL mitigation' conditions are met, then RIM DL mitigated slots are determined as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29892\_replaced([11161067](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL mitigated slots for manually triggered DL muting'.
* Else [End CB015505-A] if any of the following checks are fulfilled:
* [CB015505-A] [11163496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'Manually triggered DL mitigation' conditions are met or [End CB015505-A]
* [11163466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'Determine DL mitigation on RIM-RS detection' conditions are met or
* [11163514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'Determine DL mitigation based on RI detection' conditions are met or
* [11163530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'Determine DL mitigation based on mixed RIM-RS and RI detection' conditions are met, then:

RIM DL mitigated slots are determined in the following way:

* If actPartialSlotMuting = False then as described in [12642729: Determine RIM DL mitigated slots with whole slot granularity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HHEKcEHiEfC6a_agjpBoXg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* Else actPartialSlotMuting = True then as described in [12642924: Determine RIM DL mitigated slots with partial slot granularity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AFNpkEHoEfC6a_agjpBoXg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)​
* Else no RIM DL mitigated slots are determined.

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11161067`)

DL scheduling
Determine RIM DL mitigated slots for manually triggered DL muting

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13432358`)

DL scheduling
Note: since CB015505, this requirement is no longer maintained, as it is covered by common algorithm, see references in [11161055: Determine RIM DL mitigated slots](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

[Before CB015505-A]

If all trigger conditions described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25962\_replaced([11163496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Manually triggered DL mitigation' are fulfilled, L2PS shall determine RIM DL mitigated slots as described below:

* if rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "1:special slot muting"

> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following condtiions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

* else if rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "2:DL+special slots muting",

> PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
>
> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following condtiions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

* else if rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "3:2DL+special slots muting",

> PDSCH in the last preceding 2 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
>
> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following condtiions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

* else if rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "4:3DL+special slots muting",

> PDSCH in the last preceding 3 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
>
> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following condtiions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

* else, no slot of PDSCH shall be mitigated

[End CB015505-A]

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12642377`)

DL scheduling
Note: since CB014153-B, this requirement is no longer maintained, as it is covered by common RIM-RS/RI algorithm described in [12642729: Determine RIM DL mitigated slots with whole slot granularity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HHEKcEHiEfC6a_agjpBoXg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

* if *maxRSSymbolDistance is not higher than x of BIx y ,*

> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  ("1:DL+special slots muting" or "2:2DL+special slots muting"[CB014153-A] or "3:3DL+special slots muting" [End CB014153-A]),

> >

> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>

>
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "2:2DL+special slots muting" [CB014153-A] or "3:3DL+special slots muting" [End CB014153-A],
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding 2 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
> >

> > >

>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "1:DL+special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "0:special slots muting",
>

> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

[CB014153-A]

* else if *maxRSSymbolDistance is higher than 28+x (see x in BIx y),*

>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding 3 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated

>

>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "1:DL+special slots muting",
>

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11161090`)

DL scheduling
Determine RIM DL mitigated slots for RI or mixed RI/RIM-RS based DL muting

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12642383`)

DL scheduling
Note: since CB014153-B, this requirement is no longer maintained, as it is covered by common RIM-RS/RI algorithm described in [12642729: Determine RIM DL mitigated slots with whole slot granularity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HHEKcEHiEfC6a_agjpBoXg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[Before CB014153-B]

If all trigger conditions described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25980\_replaced([11163514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine DL mitigation based on RI detection' are fulfilled, then:

L2PS shall assume maxDlMitigationSymbol = RIEndSymbol (*see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9651\_replaced([11161729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and determine RIM DL mitigated slots as described below.*

Else if all trigger conditions described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25961\_replaced([11163530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine DL mitigation based on mixed RIM-RS and RI detection' are fulfilled, then:

L2PS shall assume maxDlMitigationSymbol = *max[RIEndSymbol(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9651\_replaced([11161729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), maxRSSymbolDistance (see in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13204\_replaced([11163050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))] and determine RIM DL mitigated slots as described below.*

* if *maxDlMitigationSymbol  is not higher than x of BIx y ,*

> PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
>
> > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> >
> > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

* else if *maxDlMitigationSymbol  is not higher than 14+x (see x in BIx y)*

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  ("1:DL+special slots muting" or "2:2DL+special slots muting"  [CB014153-A] or "3:3DL+special slots muting"  [End CB014153-A]),
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "0:special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

* else if *maxDlMitigationSymbol  is higher than 14+x [CB014153-A] and less than (28+x)[End CB014153-A] (see x in BIx y),*

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "2:2DL+special slots muting" [CB014153-A] or "3:3DL+special slots muting"  [End CB014153-A],
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding 2 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "1:DL+special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "0:special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

[CB014153-A]

* else if *maxDlMitigationSymbol  is higher than (28+x)(see x in BIx y),*

> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "3:3DL+special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding 3 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "2:2DL+special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding 2 DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "1:DL+special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in the last preceding DL slot  (DL14 ) shall be mitigated
> >
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)
>
> if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDlMutingMaxRange is  "0:special slots muting",
>
> > PDSCH in special slot  BIx y shall be mitigated if any of the following conditions are met,
> >
> > > x of BIx y is equal to 10
> > >
> > > (x of BIx y is equal to 6) AND (actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot is true)

[End CB014153-A]

* else, no slot of PDSCH shall be mitigated

[End CB014153-B]

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `12642729`)

DL scheduling
Determine RIM DL mitigated slots with whole slot granularity

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13433769`)

DL scheduling
L2PS shall determine RIM DL mitigated slots as described in below algorithm.

Inputs:

* x: number of DL symbols in special slot
* NRCELL.actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMutingMaxRange
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actPartialSlotMuting is set to False.

Algorithm:

1. Determine dlMitigationSymbolRange as described in [12642965: Determine dlMitigationSymbolRange](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aUNQkEHpEfC6a_agjpBoXg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
2. For special slot:
3. If [CB015505-A] dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 0 and [End CB015505-A] special slot either:
   1. contains 10 DL symbols or
   2. contains 6 DL symbols and actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot = true,  
      then all PDSCH symbols in special slot shall be mitigated.
4. For 1st DL slot before special slot:
5. If [Before CB015505-A-UPD001] all of the following conditions are fulfilled:
   1. rimDlMutingMaxRange = "1:DL+special slots muting" or "2:2DL+special slots muting" or "3:3DL+special slots muting" [End CB015505-A-UPD001]
   2. dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than x  
      then all PDSCH symbols in 1st DL Slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
6. For 2nd DL slot before special slot:
7. If [Before CB015505-A-UPD001] all of the following conditions are fulfilled:
   1. rimDlMutingMaxRange = "2:2DL+special slots muting" or "3:3DL+special slots muting" [End CB015505-A-UPD001]
   2. dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 14 + x  
      then all PDSCH symbols in 2nd DL Slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
8. For 3rd DL slot before special slot:
9. If [Before CB015505-A-UPD001] all of the following conditions are fulfilled:
   1. rimDlMutingMaxRange = "3:3DL+special slots muting" [End CB015505-A-UPD001]
   2. dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 28 + x  
      then all PDSCH symbols in 3rd DL Slot before special slot shall be mitigated.

Outputs:

L2PS determined which slots are mitigated when actPartialSlotMuting is disabled.

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `12642924`)

DL scheduling
Determine RIM DL mitigated slots with partial slot granularity

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13433774`)

DL scheduling
L2PS shall determine RIM DL mitigated slots as described in below algorithm.

Inputs:

* x: number of DL symbols in special slot
* NRCELL.actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMutingMaxRange
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actPartialSlotMuting is set to True.

Algorithm:

1. Determine dlMitigationSymbolRange as described in [12642965: Determine dlMitigationSymbolRange](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aUNQkEHpEfC6a_agjpBoXg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
2. For special slot:
3. If [CB015505-A] dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 0 and [End CB015505-A] special slot contains 10 DL symbols then
   1. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is less than or equal to 4, then 4 latter DL symbols of special slot shall be mitigated.
   2. Else all PDSCH symbols in special slot shall be mitigated.
4. If [CB015505-A] dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 0 and [End CB015505-A] special slot contains 6 DL symbols and actEnhancedPDSCHSchSpSlot = true, then all PDSCH symbols in special slot shall be mitigated.
5. For 1st DL slot before special slot:
6. [Before CB015505-A-UPD001] If rimDlMutingMaxRange = "1:DL+special slots muting" or "2:2DL+special slots muting" or "3:3DL+special slots muting", then [End CB015505-A-UPD001]
   1. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than x and less than or equal to x + 4, then 4 latter DL symbols of 1st DL slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
   2. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than x + 4 and less than or equal to x + 8, then 8 latter DL symbols of 1st DL slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
   3. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than x + 8, then all PDSCH symbols in 1st DL Slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
7. For 2nd DL slot before special slot:
8. [Before CB015505-A-UPD001] If rimDlMutingMaxRange = "2:2DL+special slots muting" or "3:3DL+special slots muting", then [End CB015505-A-UPD001]
   1. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 14 + x and less than or equal to 14 + x + 4, then 4 latter DL symbols of 2nd DL slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
   2. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 14 + x + 4 and less than or equal to 14 + x + 8, then 8 latter DL symbols of 2nd DL slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
   3. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 14 + x + 8, then all PDSCH symbols in 2nd DL Slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
9. For 3rd DL slot before special slot:
10. [Before CB015505-A-UPD001] If rimDlMutingMaxRange = "3:3DL+special slots muting", then [End CB015505-A-UPD001]
    1. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 28 + x and less than or equal to 28 + x + 4, then 4 latter DL symbols of 3rd DL slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
    2. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 28 + x + 4 and less than or equal to 28 + x + 8, then 8 latter DL symbols of 3rd DL slot before special slot shall be mitigated.
    3. If dlMitigationSymbolRange is greater than 28 + x + 8, then all PDSCH symbols in 3rd DL Slot before special slot shall be mitigated

Outputs:

L2PS determined which slots are mitigated when actPartialSlotMuting is enabled.

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-7**  (ID: `12642965`)

DL scheduling
Determine dlMitigationSymbolRange

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `13432383`)

DL scheduling
[CB015505-A]

L2PS shall assume dlMitigationSymbolRange according to the below algorithm.

[CB015505-A-UPD001]   
Inputs:

* mitigationFromRI (see [13482593: Mitigation symbols reduction for RI/RIM-RS detection algorithms](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaqkz8FEfG0jPRAdLhzvA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* mitigationFromRimRS  (see [13482593: Mitigation symbols reduction for RI/RIM-RS detection algorithms](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaqkz8FEfG0jPRAdLhzvA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* mitigationFromManualTrigger (see [13432384: Mitigation symbols calculation from NRRIM profile parameters](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aDWAAx7VEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* mitigationFromActInitiation (see [13432384: Mitigation symbols calculation from NRRIM profile parameters](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aDWAAx7VEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

Algorithm:  
[End CB015505-A-UPD001]

If all trigger conditions described in [13432613: Determine manually triggered with RIM-RS based DL mitigation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_i-Vupx7hEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) are fulfilled, then:

[Before CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{maxRSSymbolDistance; mitigationFromManualTrigger}  
[CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{mitigationFromRimRS; mitigationFromManualTrigger}  
[End CB015505-A-UPD001]

Else if all trigger conditions described in [13432617: Determine manually triggered with RI based DL mitigation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_KPbIYR7iEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) are fulfilled, then:

[Before CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{RIEndSymbol; mitigationFromManualTrigger}   
[CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{mitigationFromRI; mitigationFromManualTrigger}   
[End CB015505-A-UPD001]

Else if all trigger conditions described in [13432621: Determine manually triggered with mixed RIM-RS & RI based DL mitigation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Rqo8wh7iEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) are fulfilled, then:

[Before CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{RIEndSymbol; maxRSSymbolDistance; mitigationFromManualTrigger}.  
[CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{mitigationFromRI; mitigationFromRimRS; mitigationFromManualTrigger}.  
[End CB015505-A-UPD001]

Else if all trigger conditions described in [11163496: Manually triggered DL mitigation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) are fulfilled, then:

dlMitigationSymbolRange = mitigationFromManualTrigger

Else [End CB015505-A] If all trigger conditions described in [11163466: Determine DL mitigation on RIM-RS detection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) are fulfilled, then:

[Before CB015505-A]   
dlMitigationSymbolRange = maxRSSymbolDistance as determined in [11163050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).  
[Before CB015505-A-UPD001]  
[CB015505-A]   
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{maxRSSymbolDistance; mitigationFromActInitiation}   
[End CB015505-A]   
[CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{mitigationFromRimRS; mitigationFromActInitiation}   
[End CB015505-A-UPD001]

Else If all trigger conditions described in [11163514: Determine DL mitigation based on RI detection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) are fulfilled, then:

[Before CB015505-A]   
dlMitigationSymbolRange = RIEndSymbol (see [11161729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  
[Before CB015505-A-UPD001]  
[CB015505-A]   
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{RIEndSymbol; mitigationFromActInitiation}   
[End CB015505-A]   
[CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{mitigationFromRI; mitigationFromActInitiation}  
[End CB015505-A-UPD001]

Else if all trigger conditions described in [11163530: Determine DL mitigation based on mixed RIM-RS and RI detection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) are fulfilled, then:

[Before CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{RIEndSymbol(see [11161729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); maxRSSymbolDistance (see [11163050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); [CB015505-A] mitigationFromActInitiation [End CB015505-A] }.  
[CB015505-A-UPD001]  
dlMitigationSymbolRange = max{mitigationFromRI; mitigationFromRimRS; mitigationFromActInitiation}.  
[End CB015505-A-UPD001]

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-8**  (ID: `13432384`)

DL scheduling
Mitigation symbols calculation from NRRIM profile parameters

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `13432386`)

DL scheduling
The L2PS shall calculate two distinct mitigation values in symbols, derived from specific NRRIM profile parameters, as described in the algorithm below

Inputs:

* x: number of DL symbols in special slot
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMitigationManualTrigger
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimMitigationInitiation

Algorithm:  
The L2PS shall determine the following mitigation values by applying the common calculation logic described below:

* mitigationFromManualTrigger: derived from NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMitigationManualTrigger.
* mitigationFromActInitiation: derived from NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimMitigationInitiation

The calculation logic for a given parameter value is:

* If the parameter value is 0 or not available, the mitigation value is 0.
* If the parameter value is 1, the mitigation value is x.
* If the parameter value is 2, the mitigation value is x + 14.
* If the parameter value is 3, the mitigation value is x + 28.
* If the parameter value is 4, the mitigation value is x + 42.

Outputs:  
The L2PS calculated mitigationFromManualTrigger and mitigationFromActInitiation.

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-9**  (ID: `13482593`)

DL scheduling
Mitigation symbols reduction for RI/RIM-RS detection algorithms

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-3.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `13482594`)

DL scheduling
The L2PS shall calculate two distinct mitigation values, mitigationFromRI and mitigationFromRimRS, expressed in symbols. These values are derived from the RI and RIM-RS detection algorithms, respectively, according to the following procedure.

Inputs:

* x: number of DL symbols in special slot
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMutingMaxRange
* maxRSSymbolDistance: The maximum symbol distance for Reference Signal detection (see [11163050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for details).
* RIEndSymbol: The ending symbol for the RI detection (see [11161729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for details).

Algorithm:

1. Initialize Mitigation Values:
2. mitigationFromRI is initially set to RIEndSymbol.
3. mitigationFromRimRS is initially set to maxRSSymbolDistance.
4. Apply Common Calculation Logic: The following logic is applied to both mitigationFromRI and mitigationFromRimRS (referred to as currentMitigationValue in this step):
5. If NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMutingMaxRange is not available the currentMitigationValue is set to 0.
6. Else if NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMutingMaxRange is 0:
   * If currentMitigationValue is greater than x, then currentMitigationValue is reduced to x.
7. Else if NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMutingMaxRange is 1:
   * If currentMitigationValue is greater than x + 14, then currentMitigationValue is reduced to x + 14.
8. Else if NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMutingMaxRange is 2:
   * If currentMitigationValue is greater than x + 28, then currentMitigationValue is reduced to x + 28.
9. Else if NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMutingMaxRange is 3:
   * If currentMitigationValue is greater than x + 42, then currentMitigationValue is reduced to x + 42.

Outputs:  
The L2PS shall output the calculated mitigationFromRI and mitigationFromRimRS values.

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11161102`)

DL scheduling
RIM DL muting

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11161107`)

DL scheduling
Evaluation of conditional DL muting

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12654617`)

DL scheduling
gNB-DU shall evaluate the following conditions:

* If NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimSoftDlMuting is set to true and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29691\_replaced([11161193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSsm_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘Evaluation if cell load is above threshold’ results with true, then the evaluation of conditional DL muting result is ‘No DL muting’.
* Else if NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimPowerReduction is set to true and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29691\_replaced([11161193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSsm_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘Evaluation if cell load is above threshold’ results with true and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29884\_replaced([11161168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSslvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘RIM DL muting fallback timer’ has not expired, then the evaluation result is ‘No DL muting’.
* [CB014157-A] Else if NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRiPilotDlMute is set to true and RI pilot processing determine as  ‘No DL muting’. [End CB014157-A]
* Otherwise, evaluation result is ’DL muting’.

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11161119`)

DL scheduling
Determine RIM DL muting applicability

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12646503`)

DL scheduling
L2PS shall apply RIM DL muting [Before CB014153-B] for RIM mitigated slots [CB014153-B] to slots for which either: all PDSCH symbols are mitigated or only 4 or 8 latter PDSCH symbols are mitigated [End CB014153-B]  as defined in [11161055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'Determine RIM DL mitigated slots', when all of the following conditions are fulfilled:

* [11160950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3bfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'Evaluation of DL mitigation' results with true and
* [11161107](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'Evaluation of conditional DL muting' results with 'DL muting'

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11161131`)

DL scheduling
Execute RIM DL muting

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `13432645`)

DL scheduling
If the conditions described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29888\_replaced([11161119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFjPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL muting applicability' are fulfilled and after the successful fallback to default SSSG (SSSG-0) of all UEs configured with more than one SSSG, then:

·    In mitigated slots for which all PDSCH symbols are mitigated (as determined [11161055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2PS shall not schedule UE dedicated PDSCH transmission according to limitations described in [11174311](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuat-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'RIM DL muting restrictions for DL scheduling'.

·    In partially mitigated slots, for which 4 or 8 latter PDSCH symbols are mitigated, L2PS shall schedule UE dedicated PDSCH transmission according to limitations described in [12646511: Restrictions for RIM DL partial slot muting](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI__aOpckLEEfCH-cG2YrVgkA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

·    The DL slot or the special slot where exists DL symbols used for RIM RS transmission (see [11117793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall NOT be muted.

·    Mute PDCCH symbols as defined in [13242857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2uvgIMKhEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) [Before CB015505-A] and [13242859](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jt_WkMKiEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) [End CB015505-A], K2 shall be adjusted dynamically as specified in [11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Note: it is calculated during the generation of the next PDCCH slot pattern (see [11169142](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [11362969](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc_m4vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) after PDCCH DL mitigation status change.

·    If NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is set to value other than "0:disabled", then:

-    gNB shall cancel the active fault-7535 regarding RIM DL mitigation.

-    If timer NRRIM\_PROFILE.minDlMitigationDurationWoRi is not expired, then it shall be stopped.

-    If RI state 2a is false, timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi (defined by /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDlMitigationDurationWoRi) shall not be started.

·    gNB-DU shall check/determine if PDCCH and PDSCH on special slot and its preceding DL slot is muted when starting DL mitigation as described in [11161055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'Determine RIM mitigated slots'. Depending on the result of this check, a fault shall be reported, see Note 1.

·    L2PS shall keep DL muting running until DL mitigation cancel conditions are met ([11163548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Notes:

1. The fault is reported by L3, refer to [11230036](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyri7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for fault specification guidelines

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `12646511`)

DL scheduling
**Restrictions for RIM DL partial slot muting**

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13455081`)

DL scheduling
In the RIM partially mitigated slots, for which 4 or 8 latter PDSCH symbols are mitigated where RIM DL muting shall be applied (i.e.: [11161119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFjPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) ‘Determine RIM DL muting applicability’ conditions are fulfilled) PDSCH transmission shall be additionally restricted to not overlap with muted symbols of the slot. In particular, if there is no proper SLIV available, PDSCH transmission shall not be scheduled in such slot.

The following traffic type shall be scheduled without mentioned restriction: SIBs, Paging, Msg2, Msg4.

If RIM DL muting shall be applied for 4 or 8 latter PDSCH symbols of the slot and the NRRIM\_PROFILE.highPrioRbTransInMutedSlots is set to true, then additionally any UE with transmission including request class equal to or higher than gbrTraffic (see [11174018](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) 'Full list of TD resource request class priorities') can be scheduled without mentioned restriction.  
[CB014699-E-UPD001] Critical non-GBR traffic during Step1(see [13404773](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_rJo3eQyeEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) can be scheduled without mentioned restriction [End CB014699-E-UPD001].

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-5**  (ID: `11161142`)

DL scheduling
DL muting state report via fault or CM parameter

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11161147`)

DL scheduling
If NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/dlMutingStateReport is configured to 0, gNB-DU shall disable DL muting state reporting via fault-7535 or CM parameter NRCELL/[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO[End CB014133-A-UPD002]/dlMutingState.

Else if NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/dlMutingStateReport is configured to 1, gNB-DU shall support to report DL muting state via CM parameter NRCELL/[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO[End CB014133-A-UPD002]/dlMutingState periodically, the reporting interval is equal to [Before CB014133-A-UPD002]rdRiUpdateInterval (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32375\_replaced([11163858](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktcdkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \* [End CB014133-A-UPD002]NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow.

Else if NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/dlMutingStateReport is configured to 2[CB014133-A-UPD002] and NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimSoftDlMuting is false and NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPowerReduction is false[End CB014133-A-UPD002], gNB-DU shall support to report DL muting state via fault-7535 periodically, the reporting interval is equal to [Before CB014133-A-UPD002]rdRiUpdateInterval \* [End CB014133-A-UPD002]NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow.

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11161152`)

DL scheduling
RIM DL power reduction

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11161157`)

DL scheduling
Determine RIM DL power reduction applicability

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12643007`)

DL scheduling
L2PS shall apply RIM DL power reduction [Before CB014153-B] for RIM mitigated slots [CB014153-B] to slots for which either: all PDSCH symbols are mitigated or only 4 or 8 latter PDSCH symbols are mitigated [End CB014153-B] as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29890\_replaced([11161055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL mitigated slots', when all of the following conditions are fulfilled:

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29886\_replaced([11160950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3bfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Evaluation of DL mitigation' results with true,
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimPowerReduction is set to true.

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11161168`)

DL scheduling
RIM DL muting fallback timer

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11161172`)

DL scheduling
L2PS shall maintain timer for fallback to RIM DL muting. The timer shall be started (if not already started and not expired), when 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29878\_replaced([11161157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSslPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL power reduction' conditions are fulfilled. The timer shall be started for duration defined by NRRIM\_PROFILE.dlMutingFallbackTimer. [CB012719-B-UPD002] The timer shall be cleared, when any of the 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29878\_replaced([11161157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSslPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL power reduction' conditions is not met. [End CB012719-B-UPD002]

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11161178`)

DL scheduling
Determine RIM DL power reduction parameters for transmission

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11161184`)

DL scheduling
L2PS shall determine UE power reduction, **[CB012719-B] TA and MCS threshold** [End CB012719-B] limitations values according to the following rules:\*\*\*\*

* Limitations are applied from NRRIM\_PWR\_PROFILE instance pointed by the highest priority DRB for which data is contained in the buffer for UE. **[PR813934]Priorities between DRB traffic are compared according to rules of inclusion in the Transport Block specified  in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4537\_replaced([11185465](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTew_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), i.e.**
* SRB (note that presence of SRB automatically means, that no power backoff is applied, so there is no need to differentiate between SRBs)
* DRBs of  5QI5/69 (see also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4543\_replaced([11185517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTez_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* DRBs of dcGbrTraffic (see also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30517\_replaced([11185540](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvUF0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* 5QI1/65/66  voipTraffic (see also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4545\_replaced([11185562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvUF1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* 5QI1/65/66 deprioritizedVoip (see also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4545\_replaced([11185562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvUF1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* gbrTraffic request class (see also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8033\_replaced([11179713](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku6dO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* non-GBR DRBs within drbTraffic request class (see also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4178\_replaced([11174242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuaG5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* all remaining DRBs including congestion deprioritized GBR DRBs,  non-GBR DRBs with the drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class, and/or deprioritized GBR DRBs, and/or deprioritizedGbr traffic request class (see also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4550\_replaced([11185672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvUs7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* If there is more than one DRB with non-zero buffer in the highest priority class S for which DRBs with non-zero buffer are present, backoff is the lowest among backoffs assigned to these DRBs in class S. **[End PR813934][PR817790]In these conditions:**
* TA threshold shall be selected as the lowest of the TA thresholds assigned to the DRBs with non-zero buffer in the highest priority class S for which DRBs with non-zero buffer are present
* MCS threshold shall be selected as the highest of the MCS thresholds assigned to the DRBs with non-zero buffer in the highest priority class S for which DRBs with non-zero buffer are present **[End PR817790]**
* Whenever DRB does not have specified reduction or non-DRB type of **[Before** PR813934] high priority traffic is present. Meaning, any traffic after excluding the following request classes defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9891\_replaced([11174018](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Full list of TD resource request class priorities':\*\*\*\*
* voipTraffic or any lower priority traffic
* harq retransmission for any of the above traffic types

The following values are assumed: **[PR813934]**

traffic is available for the transmission for the UE, it is assumed that for the transmission:

**[End PR813934]**

* Power reduction is equal to 0.
* **[CB012719-B] MCS threshold is equal to 0.** [End CB012719-B]\*\*\*\*
* **[CB012719-B] TA threshold is considered as infinite.** [End CB012719-B]\*\*\*\*

Power reduction due to RIM determined for the transmission UE i in the cell (carrier) j in the slot t is referred as *rrmRimDLPowerReduction[i,j,t]. Whenever the context clearly binds slot, UE and cell simple* rrmRimDLPowerReduction (without indices) is used.\*\*

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `12562993`)

DL scheduling
RIM RI pilot based DL muting

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12584508`)

DL scheduling
Applicability of RI pilot processing

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-6.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13485511`)

DL scheduling
13485511:
DL scheduling
If NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRiPilotDlMute is set to true,

* and when NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is equal to ‘disabled’,
* and when conditional downlink mitigation is triggered by[11160950: Evaluation of RIM DL mitigation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3bfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9),
* and during the phase of "DL muting" as[11161107: Evaluation of conditional DL muting](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9),
* and ( [Before 05613403-26R3] NRBTS/NRCELL-tmpParam7 [05613403-26R3] NRRIM\_PROFILE.RiPilotMode [End 05613403-26R3] is "2: withRiDetectionOnly"   
  = true or no RIM RS 1 was detected (i.e. RI state2b=false, [11163032: Determination of RIM RS detected](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) ),
* and (If [Before 05613403-26R3] NRCELL-tmpParam7 [05613403-26R3] NRRIM\_PROFILE.RiPilotMode [End 05613403-26R3] is NOT  "3:postDetection" or
* no RI detection (RI state2a=false)
* and (no RIM RS 1 was detected OR if the number of detected RIM-RS type 1 setIDs in the setID list is less than NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numDetectedSetIdForMitigation, )

gNB-DU shall apply RI pilot processing. Otherwise,  gNB-DU shall stop applicability of RI pilot processing.

RI pilot processing include:

* gNB-DU shall apply "no DL muting" for each RI pilot window.
* during RI pilot window, gNB-DU shall detect RI appearance situation (see [12562998: Determination of RI appearance in pilot window](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_hSaasCrxEfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) )
* gNB-DU shall determine RIM DL muting state for next RI pilot period (see[12584537: Determine DL muting in RI pilot period](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_h-uhIDVEEfCKaNlcHOQWmg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) except its RI pilot window.
* where
* RI pilot period is the time duration of every Nx 1024SFNs, with the index range from MOD(SFN, Nx 1024)=0 to MOD(SFN, Nx 1024)=  (N-1)x 1024 , where N is given by NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/riPilotPeriod
* RI pilot window is the last Mx SFNs in each RI pilot period, with the index from MOD(SFN, M)=0 to MOD(SFN, M)= (M-1) , where M is given by NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/riPilotWindow.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a visual representation of data segmentation or partitioning. It consists of three horizontal rows, each depicting a sequence of numbered blocks.
