---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `12584537`)

DL scheduling
Determine DL muting in RI pilot period

---

**3.21.1.0-3.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12652913`)

DL scheduling
During the applicability of RI pilot processing (see [12584508: Applicability of RI pilot processing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CqX0wTVBEfCKaNlcHOQWmg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) , upon the RI detection result in the RI pilot window by[12562998: Determination of RI appearance in pilot window](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_hSaasCrxEfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) , gNB-DU shall determine DL muting state as below for the incoming RI pilot period except its RI pilot window part (see [12584508: Applicability of RI pilot processing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CqX0wTVBEfCKaNlcHOQWmg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)):

if RI disappearance in the RI pilot window [05465629] for continuous N Ri pilot windows (N is given by NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/NumOfRiPilotWindowSample ) [End 05465629] , gNB-DU shall determine as "no DL muting" state.

else if RI appearance in the RI pilot window, gNB-DU shall determine as "DL muting" state until it was finally determined by other criteria in [11161107: Evaluation of conditional DL muting](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) .

---

### 3.21.1.0-4 DL scheduling Cell load evaluation (ID: 11161188)

**3.21.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11161193`)

DL scheduling
Evaluation if cell load is above threshold

---

**3.21.1.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11161199`)

DL scheduling
When the window measurements defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29693\_replaced([11161204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSsnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Average cell load level calculations' are completed, the L2PS shall evaluate the following condition:

* If the average cell load is equal to or greater than NRRIM\_PROFILE.cellLoadThreshForRimMitigation, the evaluation result is true.
* If the average cell load is lower than NRRIM\_PROFILE.cellLoadThreshForRimMitigation, the evaluation result is false.

This evaluation result will be used until the next window measurement is completed and a new value is calculated.

Notes:

1. Due to the significant difference in time scales between the window interval and slot processing, any inaccuracies related to transient phases (e.g., a slight delay in applying the new calculated value at the window boundary) are considered negligible.

---

**3.21.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11161204`)

DL scheduling
Average cell load level calculations

---

**3.21.1.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11161212`)

DL scheduling
11161212:
DL scheduling
L2PS shall calculate average cell load level in fixed time windows, with the duration defined by NRRIM\_PROFILE.windowDurationForCellLoadAvg, according to the following formula:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
round($\frac{\sum\_{slots} PDSCH\_used\_PRBs}{\sum\_{slots} PDSCH\_available\_PRBs} \* 100\%$)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11133.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Where:

* PDSCH\_used\_PRBs is the number of PRBs used for PDSCH in a slot, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29695\_replaced([11161218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktTToPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'PRBs available for PDSCH'.
* PDSCH\_available\_PRB is the number of all available PRBs for PDSCH in a slot, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29697\_replaced([11161229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktTTovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'PRBs used for PDSCH'.
* slots are all non-UL slots included in window.

Before availability of first calculation, L2PS shall assume average cell load level equal to 0%.

---

**3.21.1.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11161218`)

DL scheduling
PRBs available for PDSCH

---

**3.21.1.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11161224`)

DL scheduling
L2PS shall determine PRBs available for PDSCH in current slot, as defined by the following requirements:

* For single BWP non-SSB & non-TRS slot, as defined in  5G\_UP\_ALG\_29708\_replaced([11177050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kusaz_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘General limitations’.
* For single BWP SSB slot, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29712\_replaced([11177132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kutB1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘General limitations’.
* For single BWP TRS slot, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29723\_replaced([11177201](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuto5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘General limitations’.
* For multi-BWP slot, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29727\_replaced([11177251](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘General limitations’.

Notes:

1. Any pooling limitations are not considered on purpose, despite the fact that pooling is enabled in current configuration.

---

**3.21.1.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `11161229`)

DL scheduling
PRBs used for PDSCH

---

**3.21.1.0-4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11161234`)

DL scheduling
L2PS shall calculate PRBs used for PDSCH in current slot as the sum of all below items:

* PRBs used for PDSCH data as distributed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4500\_replaced([11179300](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku4oDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘Resource Reservation/Allocation Sequence for Multiple UEs’.
* PRBs used for SIB1, as defined by nRbSib1 in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16705\_replaced([11164800](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kteS1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘Transport Block Size Computation’.
* PRBs used for other system information messages, as defined by nRbSibMsg in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16704\_replaced([11166021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjyXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘Transport Block Calculation’.
* PRBs used for paging, as defined by NRB in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11167889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktsVP_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ’ Step 3: determine minimum number for PRBs required for PDSCH for each slot of a PO’.

---

### 3.21.1.0-5 DL scheduling exception handling for RIM RS transmission (ID: 11161241)

**3.21.1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11161252`)

DL scheduling
According to 5G\_UP\_5389\_replaced([11360500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucvIMvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

When a slot is used for RS-1[CB009823-A] / RS-2[End CB009823-A] transmission,

* 5G-L2-PS shall stop scheduling PDSCH in this slot
* those CSI-RS for tracking, measurement or beam management transmitted on the same slot as RIM-RS transmission shall be discarded.
* When it is selected for RIM-RS downlink mitigation (5G\_UP\_5478\_replaced([11360543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucvIOfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RIM-RS shall be scheduled.
* PDCCH can be scheduled for other reasons.

---

## 3.21.2 UL scheduling

### 3.21.2.1 State machine for remote interference management

#### 3.21.2.1.0-1 State machine for remote interference management Definition of RIM session and state machine (ID: 11161269)

**3.21.2.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11161309`)

State machine for remote interference management
11161309:
State machine for remote interference management
[CB009823-A] If NRCELL-actNrRim is configured with non 0-"disable" [END CB009823-A], NR cell shall define working session containing up to 3 working states for remote interference management:

RIstate=

* 0-"noRI"  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9319\_replaced([11161316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktTTrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* 1- "suspectRI" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9320\_replaced([11161340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* 2- 2a-"RIdetected" , [Before CB009823-B] 2b-"RSdetected" [CB009823-B]2b-"RS1detected" , 2c-"RS2detected" [End CB009823-B]  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

5G-L2-PS shall control state switching for each cell. When remote interference situation is detected satisfying trigger conditions, 5G-L2-PS shall trigger RI state switching to next state (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200\_replaced([11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The state machine is illustrated on the figure below.

[Before CB009823-B]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a state diagram illustrating the Radio Interference Measurement (RIM) sessions. The diagram is divided into two main sections, representing RIM session[i] and RIM session[i+1].
**RIM session[i]:**
This section contains three states:
\* **State 0. NO\_RI:** Represented by a green circle.
\* **Self-loop:** A dashed blue circle indicates "Monitor interference in 1st UL symbol".
\* **Transition to State 1:** An arrow labeled "Interference continuously exceeds threshold" leads to State 1. Suspect\_RI.
\* **Transition out of session:** An arrow labeled "Interference NOT exceeds threshold" leads out of the RIM session[i] box.
\* **State 1. Suspect\_RI:** Represented by a yellow circle.
\* **Self-loop:** A dashed blue circle indicates "Monitor interference per UL symbol".
\* **Transition to State 2a/2b:** An arrow labeled "downhill shape appears" leads to State 2a. RI\_detected / State 2b. RS\_detected.
\* **Transition out of session:** An arrow labeled "downhill shape disappears" leads out of the RIM session[i] box.
\* **State 2a. RI\_detected / State 2b. RS\_detected:** Represented by a light blue circle.
\* **Self-loop:** A dashed blue circle indicates "Monitor RIM-RS, RI, Perform mitigation".
\* **Transition out of session:** An arrow labeled "RI and RS disappears and DL mitigation ends" leads out of the RIM session[i] box.
**RIM session[i+1]:**
This section contains one state:
\* **State 0. NO\_RI:** Represented by a green circle.
\* **Self-loop:** A dashed blue circle indicates "Monitor interference in 1st UL symbol".
\* **Transition out of session:** An arrow labeled "Interference exceeds threshold" leads out of the RIM session[i+1] box.
\* **Transition from RIM session[i]:** An arrow from State 2a/2b in RIM session[i] leads into this state.
The diagram uses dashed blue circles for monitoring actions and solid red arrows for state transitions. The overall diagram depicts a process of detecting and mitigating radio interference over consecutive RIM sessions.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11146.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB009823-B]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a state diagram illustrating the RIM (Radio Interface Monitoring) session. The diagram is divided into two main sections, representing RIM session[i] and RIM session[i+1].
**RIM session[i]**
This section contains three states:
\* **State 0. NO\_RI:** Represented by a light green circle.
\* **Action:** "Monitor interference in 1st UL symbol". This is indicated by a dashed blue circle with an arrow looping back to the state.
\* **Transition to State 1:** If "Interference continuously exceeds threshold", the system transitions to State 1.
\* **State 1. Suspect\_RI:** Represented by a yellow circle.
\* **Action:** "Monitor interference per UL symbol". This is indicated by a dashed blue circle with an arrow looping back to the state.
\* **Transition to State 2:** If "downhill shape appears", the system transitions to State 2.
\* **Transition to State 0:** If "Interference NOT exceeds threshold", the system transitions back to State 0.
\* **State 2 (composite state):** Represented by a light blue circle containing three sub-states:
\* **State 2a. RI\_detected**
\* **State 2b. RS1\_detected**
\* **State 2c. RS2\_detected**
\* **Action:** "Monitor RIM-RS 1 and 2, RI, Perform mitigation". This is indicated by a dashed blue circle with an arrow looping back to the state.
\* **Transition out of State 2:** If "RI, RS1,RS2 disappears and DL mitigation ends", the system transitions to RIM session[i+1].
**RIM session[i+1]**
This section contains one state:
\* **State 0. NO\_RI:** Represented by a light green circle.
\* **Action:** "Monitor interference in 1st UL symbol". This is indicated by a dashed blue circle with an arrow looping back to the state.
\* **Transition:** If "Interference exceeds threshold", the system transitions to the right, implying a continuation or a new session.
The diagram uses solid arrows to indicate transitions between states and dashed circles to indicate actions or monitoring activities within a state. Red lines are used to highlight specific transition conditions. The overall diagram depicts a process of detecting and mitigating interference.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11146.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[End CB009823-B]

Each RIM session defined in each NR cell shall start from RI state 0. Whether RIM session shall contain RI state 1 or RI state 2 depends on the remote interference or RIM-RS detection situation.

NR cell shall maintain a rrmRDRImonitorTimer to control the timing window (NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-NRRIMonitorWindow) used for RI monitoring in each RI state. NR cell shall maintain a counter, named rrmRDRIMsession to record the RIM session index.

RI state shall not change if NRCELL-actNrRim is reconfigured with non 0-"disable" value.

RI state shall change to RI state0 of next RIM session immediately if NRCELL-actNrRim is reconfigured to 0-"disable" .

---

#### 3.21.2.1.0-2 State machine for remote interference management RI state 0, no remote interference (ID: 11161316)

**3.21.2.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13469898`)

State machine for remote interference management
In case of NRBTS/NRCELL-actNRRIM is NOT 0.

NR cell shall enter RI state 0 in following case

- when RIM feature is activated (*actNRRIM is configured to* *NOT 0-"disable"),*\*\*

- Or, when remote interference disappears in special slot (containing guard period) and consecutive uplink slots based on corresponding RI measurements.

When NR cell enters RI state 0,

- NR cell shall de-activate existing RI alarm.

- The counter of RIM session, *rrmRDRIMsession, shall be incremented every time NR cell enters RI state 0.*

- RI Beam weight shall be updated accordingly (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9328\_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- gNB-DU shall request DU to monitor interference for configured UL symbol range after guard period with monitoring configurations (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9328\_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- [CB015735-A] If NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect=true, gNB-DU shall start and keep RIM RS detection procedure. [End CB015735-A]

NR cell shall leave RI state 0, in following cases

- when RIM feature is deactivated (actNRRIM is configured to 0). Upon deactivation of RIM feature, gNB-DU shall stop existing RIM related actions and recover to legacy mode.

NR cell shall switch to RI state 1 from RI state0 in following cases

- when RI interference is detected as suspected (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When No RI is suspected in all subbands based on 1st UL symbol after GP (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RI state shall switch to RI state 0 of next RIM session.

---

#### 3.21.2.1.0-3 State machine for remote interference management RI state 1, suspect remote interference (ID: 11161340)

**3.21.2.1.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `13469942`)

State machine for remote interference management
In case of NRBTS/NRCELL-actNRRIM is NOT 0.

NR cell shall enter RI state 1 in following case(s):

- when suspect remote interference is detected in any subband of 1st UL symbol after GP (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In RI state1, NR cell shall

- the counter of RIM session, *rrmRDRIMsession, shall remain the same as in preceding RI state 0.*

- RI Beam weight shall be determined according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31912\_replaced([11161588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

- 5G-L2-PS shall request 5G-L1-UL to monitor interference for configured UL symbol range (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9328\_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  after GP with monitoring configurations (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9328\_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **. Based on that, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate UL symbols range** impacted by RI during each RI monitoring window(i.e. NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE -*nrRiMonitorWindow)(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9651\_replaced([11161729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))*\*\*\*\*

- If fast muting SRS beam is activated (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11163368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall mute SRS based beamforming.

-  [CB015735-A] If NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect=true, gNB-DU shall start and keep RS detection procedure. [End CB015735-A]

If there are existing UL reception data in target monitoring PRB range in current subband (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9328\_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB/cell shall reuse that UL reception data to calculate RSSI, and shall not send new RI measurement request to 5G-L1-UL.

NR cell shall leave RI state 1 in following cases

- when RIM feature is deactivated (NRBTS/NRCELL-actNRRIM is configured to 0). Upon deactivation of RIM feature, 5G-L2-PS shall stop existing RIM related actions and recover to legacy mode.

- NR cell shall switch to RI state 2 when sloping shape in remote interference is detected among UL symbols in any subband and any slot with UL symbols (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). When sloping shape in remote interference is not detected among UL symbols in each subband and each slot with UL symbols (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RI state shall switch to RI state 0 of next RIM session.

---

#### 3.21.2.1.0-4 State machine for remote interference management RI state 2, remote interference is detected (ID: 11161371)

**3.21.2.1.0-4.0-7**  (ID: `13469770`)

State machine for remote interference management
NR cell shall enter RI state 2, in following cases

* RI is detected (2a=true)  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB015735-A] or RS1 is detected (2b=true) or RS2 is detected (2c=true) [End CB015735-A].
* gNB-DU shall stop the active timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi in following case
* if /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDLMitigationDurationWoRi is greater than 0 and timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi is not expired.

In RI state 2,

* NR cell shall perform same RI interference monitoring as defined for RI state 1 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9320\_replaced([11161340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* If NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimMitigationExtend = "true", gNB-DU shall determine trigger of RIM UL mitigation extension (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27175\_replaced([11163444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* gNB-DU shall trigger and keep RI mitigation actions, called “UL mitigation” (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11163368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  when following conditions are fulfilled,
* [CB015735-A] RI is detected (2a=true) AND in any of below cases: [End CB015735-A]
  + If NRBTS/NRCELL- actNrRim switch to “ 3:framework-0”  OR “4:framework-1
  + AND if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-nrRimMitigationScheme is set as  "1-UL mitigation" or "3-UL and DL mitigation"
  + Or, if NRBTS/NRCELL-actNrRim switches configured to “2:RI detection and mitigation”

- gNB-DU shall stop RI mitigation actions, called “UL mitigation” (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11163368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when following conditions are fulfilled except for fast muting SRS beam case  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11163368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

o No RI detected (2a=false)  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

o Or

§ if *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-nrRimMitigationScheme is NOT configured with  "1-UL mitigation" or "3-UL and DL mitigation";*

§ and  if *NRBTS/NRCELL-actNrRim is NOT configured to “2:RI detection and mitigation”*

- gNB-DU shall keep muting SRS based beamforming in case fast muting SRS beam is activated (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11163368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **.**

- [CB015735-A] if RI is detected (2a=true) , [End CB015735-A] gNB-DU shall determine UL symbol range impacted by RI (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9651\_replaced([11161729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- gNB-DU shall start requesting RIM RS type 1 transmission(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12735\_replaced([11160843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3ZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **in following conditions**

o if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger=**“1:constantly trigger” or “3-RS1 constantly;”*\*\*

o or

§ if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger= “2:RI trigger” OR  “4-RS2 constantly”*

§ and if RI detected (2a=true)  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- gNB-DU shall stop requesting RIM RS type 1 transmission(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12735\_replaced([11160843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3ZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in following conditions

o if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger= “2:RI trigger” OR  “4-RS2 constantly”*

o And if leave RI state 2.

- gNB-DU shall start requesting RIM RS type 2 transmission(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12735\_replaced([11160843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3ZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in following conditions

o if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger= “1:constantly trigger” or “4-RS2 constantly;”*

o or

§ if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger= “2:RI trigger” or “3-RS1 constantly”*

§ and RS1 detected (2b=true)  (see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200\_replaced([11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- gNB-DU shall stop requesting RIM RS type 2 transmission(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12735\_replaced([11160843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3ZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in following conditions

o if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsTransTrigger=  “2:RI trigger” OR “3-RS1 constantly;”*

o And if no RS1 detected (2b=false) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200\_replaced([11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- NR cell shall start and keep detecting RIM-RS procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13156\_replaced([11161857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in following conditions

o if *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE- rsDetectionWindow is NOT “0-disable”*

o And If RI detected (2a=true)  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- NR cell shall stop detecting RIM-RS procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13156\_replaced([11161857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in following conditions

o if *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE- rsDetectionWindow is “0-disable”*

o or  if leave RI state 2.

- NR cell shall manage RIM-RS based mitigation actions, called ”DL mitigation” (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13208\_replaced([11163466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25962\_replaced([11163496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25980\_replaced([11163514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25961\_replaced([11163530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- gNB-DU shall reset and start timer *maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi defined by* /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi immediately.\*\*

o if */NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi* is greater than 0 [CB015735-A]and NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect is equal to False[End CB015735-A],\*\*

o and

§ if RI state 2a becomes false,

- gNB-DU shall stop the timer *maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi in following cases*

o if */NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi is not configured,*

§ if RI state 2a becomes true before timer *maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi expires,*

§ OR if RI state 2 exits,

- gNB-DU shall reset and start timer *minDlMitigationDurationWoRi defined by* /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDlMitigationDurationWoRi  when */NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDlMitigationDurationWoRi is greater than 0.*\*\*

o if */NRBTS/NRCELL/actNrRim = ( 1 or 2)  AND (RI state 2a becomes false).*

o OR if */NRBTS/NRCELL/actNrRim = ( 3 or 4)  AND (RI state 2b is false)  AND (RI state 2a become false) after when DL mitigation is ongoing (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13208\_replaced([11163466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25962\_replaced([11163496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25980\_replaced([11163514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25961\_replaced([11163530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*

-    gNB-DU shall stop the timer *minDlMitigationDurationWoRi in following cases*

o if */NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDLMitigationDurationWoRi is greater than 0,*

§ if RI state 2a becomes true before timer *minDlMitigationDurationWoRi expires.*

§ OR if *NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is changed to false*.\*\*

NR cell shall keep in RI state 2, in following cases

- NRBTS/NRCELL-actNRRIM is configured to NOT “0:disable”

- AND

o if timer *maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi doesn’t expire* *when RI state2a is determined as false (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .*\*\*

o OR RI state 2a = true (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- And either of following conditions

o RI is detected (2a) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

o Or RS type1 is detected (2b) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200\_replaced([11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

o Or RS type2 is detected (2c)  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200\_replaced([11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

NR Cell shall leave RI state2 to RI state 0 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9180\_replaced([11161269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktTTqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in following cases

- NRBTS/NRCELL-actNRRIM is configured to “0:disable”

- Or

o if timer *maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi expires when RI state2a is determined as false (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*

o AND RI state 2a = false (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- Or

o Neither RI is detected (2a=false) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

o Nor RS type1 is detected (2b=false) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200\_replaced([11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

o Nor RS type2 is detected (2c=false) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200\_replaced([11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

when NR cell leaves RI state 2 to RI state 0 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9180\_replaced([11161269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktTTqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

- gNB-DU shall stop **RI mitigation (see see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11163368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- gNB-DU shall stop determining UL symbol range impacted by RI (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9651\_replaced([11161729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-     [CB015735-A]If NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect is equal to False, [End CB015735-A]gNB-DU shall stop requesting RIM RS type 1 transmission(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12735\_replaced([11160843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3ZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- gNB-DU shall stop requesting RIM RS type 2 transmission(see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_12735\_replaced([11160843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3ZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

-    [CB015735-A]If NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect is equal to False, [End CB015735-A]NR cell shall stop detecting RIM-RS procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13156\_replaced([11161857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- NR cell shall stop RIM-RS based mitigation actions, called ”DL mitigation”  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13208\_replaced([11163466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25962\_replaced([11163496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25980\_replaced([11163514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25961\_replaced([11163530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- NRBTS/NRCELL-actNRRIM is configured to NOT “0:disable”, RI state shall switch to 0 of next RIM session.

---

### 3.21.2.2 Request of remote interference monitoring

#### 3.21.2.2.0-1 Request of remote interference monitoring Configuration for RI measurement (ID: 11161420)

**3.21.2.2.0-1.0-8**  (ID: `11161542`)

Request of remote interference monitoring
11161542:
Request of remote interference monitoring
For each special and UL slot in one RI monitoring pattern, 5G-L2-PS shall request single RI measurement result per subband for one cell from 5G-L1-UL with following configurations :

[Before CNI-133534-C]

* 5G-L2-PS shall select patterns containing one uplink-downlink switching period followed by longer consecutive UL slots from frame structure configurations. In those patterns 5G-L2-PS can send RI monitoring request. Other patterns either containing either shorter UL duration or containing entire DL duration shall be excluded as RI monitoring patterns.

5G-L2-PS shall define a RnD parameter rdRiMonitorInterval (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10743\_replaced([11163734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to control how often the RI monitoring request shall be sent.  the values of rdRiMonitorInterval (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10743\_replaced([11163734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is {1,2,4,8} used for loading adaptation purpose at  5G-L1-UL side ,  default is 1.

Example.

[xlsx\_desc]--- Sheet1 ---
ulDlDataSlotRatio 3/7 NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN
rdRiMonitorInterval =1 NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN D D D NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN D D D
rdRiMonitorInterval =2 NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN D D D NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN
ulDlDataSlotRatio 1/4 NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN
rdRiMonitorInterval =1 NaN NaN NaN D D NaN NaN NaN D D NaN NaN NaN D D NaN NaN NaN D D
rdRiMonitorInterval =2 NaN NaN NaN D D NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN D D NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN
ulDlDataSlotRatio 2/8 NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN
rdRiMonitorInterval =1 NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN D D D NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN D D D
rdRiMonitorInterval =2 NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN D D D NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN[/xlsx\_desc][xlsx\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/attachments/m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file11172\_0.xlsx[/xlsx\_path]

[CNI-133534-C]

gNB-DU shall select TDD patterns for RI measurement per subband as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32684\_replaced([11161602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CNI-133534-C]

* Beamforming configuration containing SSB beam weight used for RI monitoring (RIM beam). [Before CNI-133534-C]Such RIM beam weight shall correspond to SSB Beam index derived for each RIM session according to the following formula:

SSB Beam Index = (rrmRDRIMsession) mod (nActivatedSsPbch)

The number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch) is defined in the 5G\_UP\_82\_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The figure below illustrates the relationship between SSB beam index and RIM session index, where example number of transmitted SSB blocks is equal to 4.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating a system's behavior over several "RIM sessions" labeled from 'i' to 'i+4'. The diagram is structured as a table with rows representing different parameters and columns representing the sessions. Below the table, a state machine diagram shows the transitions between different states.
The table has the following rows:
- **RIM session**: This row indicates the session number.
- **SSB index (e.g., 4SSB)**: This row shows an index value, represented by 'B' and a number, for each session. In session 'i', it's 'B' and '0'. In session 'i+1', it's 'B' and '1'. In session 'i+2', it's 'B' and '2'. In session 'i+3', it's 'B' and '3'. In session 'i+4', it's 'B' and '0'.
- **RI measurement state**: This row shows a numerical state for each session. Session 'i' has states '0', '1', '2'. Session 'i+1' has states '0', '1'. Session 'i+2' has states '0', '1', '2'. Session 'i+3' has states '0'. Session 'i+4' has states '0'.
- **RI mitigation (state2)**: This row indicates whether RI mitigation is active, with values 'TRUE' or 'FALSE' for each session. Session 'i' is 'TRUE'. Session 'i+1' is 'FALSE'. Session 'i+2' is 'TRUE'. Session 'i+3' is 'FALSE'. Session 'i+4' is 'FALSE'.
Below the table, a state machine diagram depicts transitions between states:
- **State 0 (No RI)**: Represented by a green circle.
- **State 1 (suspect RI)**: Represented by a yellow circle.
- **State 2 (detected RI)**: Represented by a gray circle.
Arrows indicate transitions:
- Blue arrows signify "Reuse the same beam for RI measurement".
- Red arrows signify "Need to change beam for RI measurement".
The state machine shows the following sequence of states and transitions:
- State 0 (No RI) transitions to State 1 (suspect RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 1 (suspect RI) transitions to State 2 (detected RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 2 (detected RI) transitions to State 0 (No RI) via a red arrow.
- State 0 (No RI) transitions to State 1 (suspect RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 1 (suspect RI) transitions to State 0 (No RI) via a red arrow.
- State 0 (No RI) transitions to State 1 (suspect RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 1 (suspect RI) transitions to State 2 (detected RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 2 (detected RI) transitions to State 0 (No RI) via a red arrow.
- State 0 (No RI) transitions to State 0 (No RI) via a red arrow.
Dashed lines connect specific points in the table to the state machine diagram, indicating how the table values influence the state transitions. For example, the 'RI measurement state' values in session 'i' (0, 1, 2) correspond to the initial sequence of states in the state machine. The 'RI mitigation (state2)' values also seem to correlate with the transitions.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11172.002.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CNI-133534-C] gNB-DU shall configure RIM Beam as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31912\_replaced([11161588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

note: regarding TDD pattern selection and RIM Beam configuration, gNB-DU shall switch RIM beam every Nframe radio frames during RI state0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9319\_replaced([11161316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktTTrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), where Nframe =Number of subbands \* roundup(rdRiMonitorInterval/2)) when rdRiMonitorSubband="1-single subband" and Nframe =roundup(rdRiMonitorInterval/2)) when rdRiMonitorSubband(see in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29863\_replaced([11163755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))="2-all subbands" .   [End CNI-133534-C]

Note: the RI beam weight is required only for blank RBs and symbols in case beamforming is configured

* RI monitoring PRB region of each sub-band containing start RI PRB index (RIstartPRB) and number of RI PRBs(rdRImonitorPRB ).

The RI monitoring PRB region shall be selected from the selection range which starts from the PRB index equal to ( nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL + subband\_index \*  rdRIMsubbandsize ), and ends at the PRB index equal to min((subband\_index+1) \*  rdRIMsubbandsize-1, maxUlPRBindex  -nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL)

where

* rdRIMsubbandsize for RI monitoring shall be set at 20MHz, containing PRB number determined by subcarrier spacing(SCS), i.e. for SCS 15kHz, rdRIMsubbandsize = 110PRBs, for 30kHz - 55PRBs.

Note: The rest subband shall be used without enough RB, e.g. 10MHz of rest bandwidth for cases of chBw is odd \* 10MHz

* maxUlPRBindex is maximum index of uplink PRB
* nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL and nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL are defined as in the 5G\_UP\_362\_replaced([11349089](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubbgqvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Number of RI PRBs is 6 .

Within the PRB selection range in the primary subcell, 5G-L2-PS shall select consecutive 6 PRB from 1)scheduled PRBs in RIM-RS detection element, 2)scheduled PRBs for PUSCH and apSRS, 3) scheduled PRBs for PUSCH, 4) scheduled PRBs for apSRS, 5) unused PRBs for PUSCH/apSRS/RIM-RS, excluding the region of PUCCH and PRACH.

RIstartPRB is the first PRB index of the selected 6 PRB region

The UL symbol of special slot where pSRS is present shall be handled as scheduled region for RI measurement and the first and the last PRBs on this slot shall be excluded except last two symbols in UL slots .

[Before CNI-133534-C]

* gNB-DU shall repeat looping all subbands orderly and select number of subbands for RI monitoring request (rdRiMonitorSubband, see in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29863\_replaced([11163755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in each selected TDD pattern.The example with rdRiMonitorSubband=1 and rdRiMonitorInterval=1 in case of ulDlDataSlotRatio = 1/4 is as below:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image displays a grid-like structure with colored blocks and white lines. The top row contains a few colored blocks: a white block, a yellow block, and a blue block. Below this, a row of colored blocks is arranged in a repeating pattern of blue, white, yellow, and blue. This pattern appears to be a sequence of blocks. The rest of the image is filled with a grid of white lines on a black background, creating cells. There are no discernible objects, text, or meaningful patterns within the grid itself. The colored blocks at the top seem to be a key or legend for the grid, but their exact meaning is not clear from the image alone.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11172.003.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[End CNI-133534-C]

If actNRRIM is configured to 1 or 2,  5G-L2-PS shall allocate 2 streams with streamIndex = {0,1} for RI measurement request.

If actNRRIM is configured to 3 and if RI measurements is requested in the same target slot with RIM-RS, it shall use same streams as RIM-RS in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13206\_replaced([11162604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and shall be performed based on the data in RIM-RS region (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13156\_replaced([11161857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* With slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RI monitoring PRBs from the unscheduled PRB regions, if any, can be used only if there are still sufficient PRBs left from the total usable PRBs available in the slot for the PUSCH area and this limit is not going to be exceeded (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* UL symbol range to be monitored, in terms of start UL symbol index and number of symbols, where start UL symbol index is determined by RI state and slot configuration:

> If (NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimRssiMeasInState0 is equal to 0) and (gNB is in RI state 0), start UL symbol index shall be equal to first UL symbol index determined by TDD slot format (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
>
> Else, it shall be all UL symbols including last two symbols of the UL slot considering the PRB range of existing aperiodic SRS (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16799\_replaced([11161550](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhyvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* Uplink slot index i: i=0 for special slot, i=1 to N for 1st and up to Nth consequent UL slot respectively. N is determined by longest consecutive UL slots number in the used slot pattern

#### 3.21.2.2.0-2 Request of remote interference monitoring Computation of PRB range of aperiodic SRS (ID: 11161550)

**3.21.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11161581`)

Request of remote interference monitoring
11161581:
Request of remote interference monitoring
5G-L2-PS shall derive the scheduled PRB range of aperiodic SRS used for RRC connected user via computing startPrb and numRbg based on the detail SRS Configuration Data refers to "SRS-Config" in section 6.3.2, 3GPP 38.331.

The computation shall be done as following wideband SRS configurations

SRS  Wideband settings for SU-MIMO:

 b-SRS set to 0,

 b-hop set to 0,

 [image-0][image\_desc]startPrb = n\_shift + K\_TC \* W\_sc,0^SRS \* n\_q[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11174.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

- [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a white background. The equation is:
$n\_0 = \lfloor 4m\_{RRC}/m\_{SRS,0} \rfloor \mod N\_0$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11174.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]with [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "m SRS, O" with a slight blur and a colorful gradient effect on the letters.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11174.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] and N0 from table below

-  [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a black background. The equation is:
$W\_{sc,0}^{SRS} = m\_{SRS,0} / K\_{TC}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11174.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

 [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a dark font against a light, slightly blurred background. The equation reads: numRbg = mSRS,0 / 4. The text is in a sans-serif font. The 'm' in 'mSRS,0' is slightly smaller than the other letters and appears to be a subscript. The '0' is also a subscript. The division symbol is a forward slash.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11174.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a table with 7 rows and 7 columns. The first column is labeled "C\_SRS" and contains numerical values. The remaining columns are grouped by "Bsrs" values: 0, 1, 2, and 3. Each "Bsrs" group has two sub-columns: "m\_SRS,x" and "Nx", where 'x' corresponds to the Bsrs value.
Here is the table in markdown format:

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | m\_SRS,0 | N0 | m\_SRS,1 | N1 | m\_SRS,2 | N2 | m\_SRS,3 | N3 |
| 13 | 48 | 1 | 24 | 2 | 12 | 2 | 4 | 3 |
| 25 | 104 | 1 | 52 | 2 | 4 | 13 | 4 | 1 |
| 30 | 128 | 1 | 64 | 2 | 32 | 2 | 4 | 8 |
| 40 | 160 | 1 | 80 | 2 | 40 | 2 | 4 | 10 |
| 51 | 216 | 1 | 108 | 2 | 36 | 3 | 4 | 9 |
| 61 | 272 | 1 | 136 | 2 | 68 | 2 | 4 | 17 |

Table 1 : SRS bandwidth configuration (wideband)

5G-L2-PS shall derive unscheduled PRB range which is outside of scheduled part corresponding to startPrb and numRbg of existing aperiodic SRS in the UL slot.

#### 3.21.2.2.0-3 Request of remote interference monitoring RIM beam configuration (ID: 11161588)

**3.21.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11161596`)

Request of remote interference monitoring
11161596:
Request of remote interference monitoring
When gNB-DU requests RI measurement per symbol and per subband for one cell from 5G-L1-UL (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9328\_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* If rdRiMonitorAllSsb="1" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31909\_replaced([11163711](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall request RSSI measurement configured with each SSB beam,

-  If no suspect RI  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or no RI detected  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

and when gNB-DU selected available TDD pattern to request single RI measurement result per subband

o RIM beam shall configure SSB beam ID=0 when gNB-DU started first RI measurement request for subband0;

o If number of SSB >0

and when gNB-DU requests new RI measurement for subband0 in a different frame to the latest RIM beam reconfiguration,

then, gNB-DU shall reconfigure the RIM beam configuration orderly with next SSB beam ID as below

 Current RIM beam = SSB beam ID = MOD (last\_SSBBeamId +1, NRBTS/NRCELL/NRHOIF/numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks)

o gNB-DU shall keep current RIM beam for following RI measurements requests before next slot of RIM beam reconfiguration

- If suspect RI appears (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall select the worst-RI SSB beam ID (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as RIM beam to be used in following processings in current RIM session.

* else if rdRiMonitorAllSsb="0" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31909\_replaced([11163711](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall configure RIM beam for RSSI measurement with one SSB Beam ID derived for current RIM session according to the following formula: as below:

SSB Beam ID = (rrmRDRIMsession) mod (nActivatedSsPbch)

The number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch) is defined in the 5G\_UP\_82\_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and equal to numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks.

The figure below illustrates the relationship between SSB beam index and RIM session index, where example number of transmitted SSB blocks is equal to 4.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating a system's behavior over several "RIM sessions" labeled from 'i' to 'i+4'. The diagram is structured as a table with rows representing different parameters and columns representing the sessions. Below the table, a state machine diagram shows the transitions between different states.
The table has the following rows:
- **RIM session**: This row indicates the session number.
- **SSB index (e.g., 4SSB)**: This row shows an index value, represented by 'B' and a number, for each session. In session 'i', it's 'B' and '0'. In session 'i+1', it's 'B' and '1'. In session 'i+2', it's 'B' and '2'. In session 'i+3', it's 'B' and '3'. In session 'i+4', it's 'B' and '0'.
- **RI measurement state**: This row shows a numerical state for each session. Session 'i' has states '0', '1', '2'. Session 'i+1' has states '0', '1'. Session 'i+2' has states '0', '1', '2'. Session 'i+3' has states '0'. Session 'i+4' has states '0'.
- **RI mitigation (state2)**: This row indicates whether RI mitigation is active, with values 'TRUE' or 'FALSE' for each session. Session 'i' is 'TRUE'. Session 'i+1' is 'FALSE'. Session 'i+2' is 'TRUE'. Session 'i+3' is 'FALSE'. Session 'i+4' is 'FALSE'.
Below the table, a state machine diagram depicts transitions between states:
- **State 0 (No RI)**: Represented by a green circle.
- **State 1 (suspect RI)**: Represented by a yellow circle.
- **State 2 (detected RI)**: Represented by a gray circle.
Arrows indicate transitions:
- Blue arrows signify "Reuse the same beam for RI measurement".
- Red arrows signify "Need to change beam for RI measurement".
The state machine shows the following sequence of states and transitions:
- State 0 (No RI) transitions to State 1 (suspect RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 1 (suspect RI) transitions to State 2 (detected RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 2 (detected RI) transitions to State 0 (No RI) via a red arrow.
- State 0 (No RI) transitions to State 1 (suspect RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 1 (suspect RI) transitions to State 0 (No RI) via a red arrow.
- State 0 (No RI) transitions to State 1 (suspect RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 1 (suspect RI) transitions to State 2 (detected RI) via a blue arrow.
- State 2 (detected RI) transitions to State 0 (No RI) via a red arrow.
- State 0 (No RI) transitions to State 0 (No RI) via a red arrow.

For example, the 'RI measurement state' values in session 'i' (0, 1, 2) correspond to the initial sequence of states in the state machine. The 'RI mitigation (state2)' values also seem to correlate with the transitions.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11176.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

#### 3.21.2.2.0-4 Request of remote interference monitoring Selection of TDD patterns for RI measurement (ID: 11161602)

**3.21.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11161611`)

Request of remote interference monitoring
11161611:
Request of remote interference monitoring
gNB-DU shall select available TDD pattern to request single RI measurement result per subband for one cell from DU with following configurations :

* gNB-DU shall select longer TDD patterns (which contains one uplink-downlink switching period followed by longer consecutive UL slots from frame structure configurations) and send RI monitoring request. gNB-DU shall exclude other patterns containing either shorter UL duration or entire DL duration from RI monitoring patterns.
* gNB-DU shall repeat looping all subbands orderly and select number of subbands (rdRiMonitorSubband="1-single subband" or "2-all subbands", see in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29863\_replaced([11163755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for RI monitoring request in one selected radio frame which contains available longer TDD patterns for measurement.
* gNB-DU shall define a RnD parameter rdRiMonitorInterval (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10743\_replaced([11163734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to control how often the RI monitoring request shall be sent, then gNB-DU shall send RI monitoring request in every N(=roundup(rdRiMonitorInterval /2)) TDD radio frame(s).
* The example with rdRiMonitorSubband=1 and rdRiMonitorInterval=1 in case of ulDlDataSlotRatio = 2/8 is as below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a grid-like structure, likely a calendar or schedule, spanning five rows and multiple columns. Each row is labeled with a year, starting from "2000" at the top and ending with "2004" at the bottom. Within each row, there are further subdivisions labeled "S00", "S01", "S02", and "S03".

### 3.21.2.3 Processing of RI measurement data

#### 3.21.2.3.0-1 Processing of RI measurement data Smoothing interference measurement result from L1 (ID: 11161622)

**3.21.2.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12739845`)

Processing of RI measurement data
5G-L2-PS shall smooth interference measurement result reported by 5G-L1-UL.

* The recorded values shall be smoothed using the following formula:

RI[i][symbol]=RI’[i][symbol]*(1-rdRimSmoothAlpha(5G\_UP\_ALG\_9655\_replaced([11163724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) )+RI\_L1H*rdRimSmoothAlpha(5G\_UP\_ALG\_9655\_replaced([11163724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

where i indicates slot index (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9328\_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RI’ is previously measured RI in the same slot and symbol, *rdRimSmoothAlpha (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9655\_replaced([11163724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be configurable R&D parameter, with default value of 0.1.*

* If rdRiMonitorAllSsb="1" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31909\_replaced([11163711](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall perform the smoothing per subband per configured SSB beam and per UL symbol in each slot,   
  else if rdRiMonitorAllSsb="0" ,  The **smoothing shall be performed within subband per UL symbol in each slot.**
* Smoothed record shall be reset when RI monitoring period (*NRRIMonitorWindow) restarts, initial value shall be**[Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase**[CB014613-A]defined by RI detection threshold ([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PGfkwWhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))**[End CB014613-A]*.****\****\*

[PR863062]

* (smooth for RI pilot window)When NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRiPilotDlMute = true, if the RI pilot window (given by NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/riPilotWindow) <=10, and when the the RI pilot window starts, gNB-DU shall create the separate smoothed record sets with initial value from the first measurement reports the RI pilot window.
* gNB-DU shall maintain the separate smoothed record sets using the following formula:
* RI[i][symbol]=RI’[i][symbol]*0.5+RI\_L1H*0.5
* where，i indicates slot index, RI’ is the previous measured RI in the same slot and the same symbol.

[End PR863062]

Smoothed record shall be reset when RI monitoring period (NRRIMonitorWindow) restarts, initial value shall be [Before CB014613-A]NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613]defined by RI detection threshold(12713680) [End CB014613-A].

Due to the measurement result smoothing, 5G-L2-PS shall deduce the beam ID value for the RI[i][symbol] based on below criteria:

- In case PRB range and the UL symbol index of RI\_L1H are NOT used for any UL channel during the monitoring window

Beam ID value shall be the pattern ID of RI beam **(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31912\_replaced([11161588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

- In case PRB range and the UL symbol index of RI\_L1H are from UL scheduling with same sector beam ID during the monitoring window

Beam ID value shall be the sector beam ID  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2037\_replaced([11112372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- In case PRB range and the UL symbol index of RI\_L1H are used for scheduling with different beam pattern IDs during the monitoring window

Beam ID value shall **has no value  in case no beam was used or no measurement was requested.**

---

#### 3.21.2.3.0-2 Processing of RI measurement data Determination of suspect remote interference (ID: 11161641)

**3.21.2.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12739961`)

Processing of RI measurement data
12739961:
Processing of RI measurement data
In RI state 0, 5G-L2-PS shall determine if RI is suspected in any sub-band by comparing smoothed RI measurement results with pre-defined RI threshold ([Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A][12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PLXdsGhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg)[End CB014613-A]). The RI comparison shall be performed on 1st UL symbol after GP (*InitUL) belonging to RI monitoring pattern (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9328\_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for each monitoring sub-band during RI monitoring window (*NRRIMonitorWindow).*\*\*

In the beginning of RI monitoring window, *RI\_counter[subband] shall be initialized and set to 0 for each sub-band.* RI\_counter[subband] shall count number of occurrences where interference has exceeded [Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A]the pre-defined NR threshold ([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PLXdsGhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A].* RIDetected\_subband shall be initialized and set to 0. *RIDetected\_subband shall count number of subbands impacted by high interference.*\*\*\*\*

During each RI monitoring window, per each RI comparison, the occurrence of suspect RI shall be determined by the following criteria:

The RI in *InitUL shall exceeds[Before CB014613-A]threshold of* NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A]the pre-defined NR threshold ([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PLXdsGhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A]\*\*

Each suspect RI occurrence shall be counted into *RI\_counter[subband]*

In parallel, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate number of performed suspect RI comparison (*numOfRIComparison). Those shorter consecutive UL slots of patterns shall be excluded from comparison scope. The* numOfRIComparison is same to all subbands during each monitoring window.\*\*

The time interval between the special slot and the previous special slot which performed RI comparison shall be taken into use as duration of suspect RI for current comparison, which shall be counted into total suspect RI duration result for this subband in this monitoring window, example as below

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a timeline represented by a series of colored squares arranged in two rows. The squares are colored blue, white, and yellow. Below the timeline, there are two red arrows indicating durations, with text labels associated with them.
The top row of squares shows a pattern of blue, white, and yellow squares. The bottom row of squares is mostly black, with white grid lines separating them.
The first red arrow, pointing from left to right, is labeled "Suspect RI duration". This arrow spans across a significant portion of the timeline, covering multiple blue, white, and yellow squares in the top row.
The second red arrow, also pointing from left to right, is shorter and positioned further to the right on the timeline. It is labeled "duration".
The overall impression is a visual representation of time intervals, with specific segments marked as "Suspect RI duration" and another general "duration". The colored squares likely represent different states or events within the timeline.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11185.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

At the end of each RI monitoring window, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate RISlotRatio per subband (RISlotRatio[subband]) indicating the ratio of high interference impacted slots to number of compared slots,

*i.e. RISlotRatio[subband] =* RI\_counter[subband] / numOfRIComparison\*\*

5G-L2-PS shall compare the RI slot ratio to the threshold NrRiThresDurationRatio for each subband, if [PR867168] equal to or [End PR867168]exceeds threshold, i.e.  RISlotRatio [sub-band] >[PR867168] = [End PR867168] NRCELL-NRRIthresholdDurationRatio, then suspect RI occurs in the subband. The number of occurrences subband shall be counted to *RIDetected\_subband*

- If rdRiMonitorAllSsb="1" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31909\_replaced([11163711](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall repeat above RI comparison processing for each SSB beam and get the result *for each SSB beam, i.e.* RIDetected\_subband[SSB ID]\*\*

>  If any *RIDetected\_subband[SSB ID] > 0,  gNB-DU shall determine suspect RI appears in current cell.*

> Else if all *RIDetected\_subband [SSB ID] == 0,  gNB-DU shall determine suspect RI disappears in current cell.*

**> At the end of each RI monitoring window, among all *RIDetected\_subband[SSB ID] , gNB-DU shall determine the worst-RI SSB beam ID (worstRimSsbId) \**and worst-RI Subband ID (worstRimSubbId) which has the highest smoothed RI measurement results (worstRimRSSI) on* initUL***\*\*\*

- else if rdRiMonitorAllSsb="0", then

> If *RIDetected\_subband > 0,   gNB-DU shall determine suspect RI appears in current cell. Else if* RIDetected\_subband == 0, gNB-DU shall confirm suspect RI absence.\*\*

---

#### 3.21.2.3.0-3 Processing of RI measurement data Determination of remote interference appearance (ID: 11161667)

**3.21.2.3.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `12653175`)

Processing of RI measurement data
12653175:
Processing of RI measurement data
In RI state 1 and 2, 5G-L2-PS shall determine remote interference appearance in any sub-band by comparing smoothed RI measurement results with RI threshold ([Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A][12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PLXdsGhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg)[End CB014613-A]). The comparison shall be conducted on 1st UL symbol after GP(*InitUL) belonging to RI monitoring pattern (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9328\_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , as well on 1st UL symbol of subsequent UL slots for each monitoring sub-band during RI monitoring window (*NRRIMonitorWindow).***In addition, RI level difference between two UL symbols chosen at specified positions (*NrRiMonitorDownhillStartSymbol and *NrRiMonitorDownhillEndSymbol ) in each UL slot of each RI monitoring pattern shall be compared to the drop height threshold for RI detection(*NRRIthresholdDropHeight) **, and** RI level difference between the first UL symbol and the last UL symbol in special slot \**shall be compared to* nrRiThresDropHeightSpecialSlot. Such comparison aims to determine if sloping shape occurs or not and shall be performed for each subband during each RI monitoring window(\*NRRIMonitorWindow).******\*****In the beginning of RI monitoring window,*RI\_counter[subband][slot]  shall be initialized and set to 0 and used to count number of patterns with RI occurrences for each subband during RI monitoring window. *RIDetected\_subband shall be initialized and set to 0.* RIDetected\_subband shall count number of subbands impacted by remote interference during RI monitoring window.***During each timing window, each time of RI comparison shall be performed per subband traversing special slot and all* *consecutive UL slot[i] following the* InitUL . The RI occurrence shall be determined by following criterion for RI comparing:***If the RI in* InitUL exceeds[Before CB014613-A]threshold of *NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A] the pre-defined RI threshold ([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PLXdsGhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A], then**- For UL slot i,
o If {NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiDisableMonitorPowerOfUSlot is False} AND* {The RI in 1st UL symbol of UL slot i exceeds [Before CB014613-A]threshold of *NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A] the pre-defined RI threshold ([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PLXdsGhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A]} AND {The RI difference between* NrRiMonitorDownhillStartSymbol AND *NrRiMonitorDownhillEndSymbol exceeds threshold of* NRRIthresholdDropHeight}, then***\**
 one time of RI occurrence shall be confirmed for the subband in every preceding slot (<=i) in current pattern which contains the *InitUL and UL slot i.*
o Else if {NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiDisableMonitorPowerOfUSlot is True} AND *{The RI difference between* NrRiMonitorDownhillStartSymbol and *NrRiMonitorDownhillEndSymbol exceeds threshold of* NRRIthresholdDropHeight}, then**** one time of RI occurrence shall be confirmed for the subband in every preceding slot (<=i) in current pattern which contains the *InitUL and UL slot i.*- For special slot,
o If {NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiMonitorInSSlotEnabled is True} AND {*NRCELL.tddFrameStructure.frameStructureType is equal to 'tdLte'} AND {The RI in the first UL symbol of special slot exceeds *[Before CB014613-A]threshold of* *NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A]the pre-defined RI threshold ([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_PLXdsGhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A]* } AND {The RI difference between the first UL symbol and *the last UL symbol* of special slot *exceeds threshold of* nrRiThresDropHeightSpecialSlot}, then******\*
 one time of RI occurrence shall be confirmed for the subband in the special slot (i=0)  in current pattern which contains the* InitUL.*End If
where
-* rdRiMonitorPowerOfUslot\*reference to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23688\_replaced([11163788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktb2gvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**
- *rdRiMonitorInSslot  reference to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23666\_replaced([11163773](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*
 
During monitoring time window, 5G-L2-PS shall count the number of RI occurrence for each subband and each slot ( *RI\_counter[subband] [slot]) , and the number of RI comparison (*numOfRIComparison) which is the same for all subbands.\*\*
 
 
The time interval between current RI occurrence pattern and the previous RI comparison pattern shall be taken into use as duration of RI for current comparison, which shall be count into total RI duration result for this subband in this monitoring window, an example as below
[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a table with several rows and columns, illustrating a comparison of data slots. The top row contains numerical labels from 0 to 20, representing time slots or indices. Below this, there are three rows of data.
