#### 3.21.2.3.0-4 Processing of RI measurement data Determination of RI impacted UL symbol range (ID: 11161729)

**3.21.2.3.0-4.0-5**  (ID: `12733984`)

Processing of RI measurement data
During determining remote interference appearance or disappearance in RI state 1 and 2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall calculate impacted UL symbol range start from the *end symbol of RI sloping in the latest**slot with occurrence of remote interference towards* initUL.\*\*\*\*

If NRBTS.NRCELL.NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiMonitorInSSlotEnabled = false,

* For each subband in UL slot i, when each time of RI occurrence was confirmed (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall determine the lastest RI impacted symbol by below criteria

*> if l >0,* (smoothedRI  - smoothedRI  ) > *dropStep (dB) AND smoothedRI   > [Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A]the pre-defined RI threshold([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PGfkwWhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A]*,*Or if l=0 , smoothedRI  > [Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A]the pre-defined RI threshold([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PGfkwWhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A]* (dB)***\****\*

**- For** each subband in UL slot i, **if (RI appears on UL slot i) AND (RI sloping end symbol in slot i can’t be found** with above steps), the last uplink symbol **of slot i** is treated as RI sloping end symbol.***\******\***

Else

* For each subband in UL slot i, when each time of RI occurrence was confirmed (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall determine the lastest RI impacted symbol by below criteria

*> if l >0,* (smoothedRI  - smoothedRI  ) > *dropStep (dB) AND smoothedRI   > [Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A]the pre-defined RI threshold([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PGfkwWhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A]*, Or if l=0 , smoothedRI  > [Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A]the pre-defined RI threshold([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PGfkwWhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A] *(dB)***\***\*

***\*- For* \*each subband in UL slot i, if (RI appears on slot i) AND (RI sloping end symbol in slot i can’t be found** with above steps), the last uplink symbol **of slot i** is treated as RI sloping end symbol.***\******\***

* If (RI sloping is not found in UL slots) and (NRCELL.tddFrameStructureType is equal to 'tdLte'), 5G-L2-PS shall determine the lastest RI impacted symbol on special slot by below criteria

for each subband in special slot,

*>*if l > 14-y (y is the number of uplink symbols on special slot, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), *(smoothedRI  - smoothedRI  ) >* dropStepSpecialSlot (dB) AND smoothedRI   > [Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A]the pre-defined RI threshold([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PGfkwWhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A]*, Or if l=14-y *, smoothedRI  > [Before CB014613-A]*NRRIthresholdbase[CB014613-A]the pre-defined RI threshold([12713680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PGfkwWhmEfCk8v_SG2h2xg))[End CB014613-A] *(dB)****\****\*

***\*- For* \*each subband in special slot,** if (RI appears on special slot) AND (RI sloping end symbol in slot i can’t be found **with above steps), the last uplink symbol** of special slot **is treated as RI sloping end symbol.*****\******\***

Where

* dropStep (dB) = max(0.5, *NRCELL.NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiThresDropHeight /(*NRCELL.NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiMonitorDownhillEndSymbol -*NRCELL.NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiMonitorDownhillStartSymbol) )*\*\*
* dropStepSpecialSlot (dB) = max(0.5, *NRCELL.NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiThresDropHeightSpecialSlot / y (y is the number of uplink symbols on special slot, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))))*
* the symbol *l shall be  from* NRCELL.NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiMonitorDownhillEndSymbol towards *1st*symbol in slot i\*\*\*\*

The highest value of *l (symbol) in highest value of* i (UL slot) shall be deemed as the index of lastest RI impacted UL symbol in this subband, symbol range from initUL to this symbol  *shall be deemed as impacted by RI in this subband and shall be counted for each symbol .*\*\*

At the end of each RI monitoring window(*NRRIMonitorWindow), 5G-L2-PS shall calculate the ratio of RI for each UL symbol , RIsymbolRatio(subband,i,l). Among those UL symbols with RIsymbolRatio(subband,l) > NrRiThresDurationRatio, the highest value of l (symbol) in highest value of i (UL slot) shall be determined as* RIEndSymbol [subband] which indicates the end of RI sloping, , in this subband.\*\*

At the end of RI monitoring window,

* if RI is confirmed appearance (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

> 5G-L2-PS shall calculate the result of *RIEndSymbol [subband]. The highest value of  among all* RIEndSymbol [subband] shall be determined as final result of *RIEndSymbol in term of* .\*\*\*\*

> 5G-L2-PS shall calculate length of RI impacted UL symbol range (RIImpactedLength) with number of UL symbols from *initUL untill* RIEndSymbol (=*)after guard period.*\*\*

> [CB014157-A] in case RI appearance due to RI detected in pilot window (see [11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU shall keep using the last *RIEndSymbol and RIImpactedLength. [End CB014157-A]*

* else if RI is confirmed disappearance (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

> set *RIEndSymbol  to* initUL-1 , and set RIImpactedLength  to 0.\*\*

---

#### 3.21.2.3.0-5 Processing of RI measurement data Determination of high RSSI on initial UL symbol (ID: 11161754)

**3.21.2.3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13439077`)

Processing of RI measurement data
If *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-fastMuteSrsBeamForRi= true, gNB-DU shall determine if there is high RSSI on first UL symbol of s-slot (HighRSSI\_initUL) by comparing the smoothed RI measurement results with pre-defined RI threshold. The RI comparison shall be performed on 1st UL symbol after GP (InitUL) belonging to RI monitoring pattern (see [11161420: Configuration for RI measurement](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_7RvYoPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for each monitoring sub-band during RI monitoring window (NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/NRRIMonitorWindow).*

In the beginning of RI monitoring window, HighRssi\_counter[subband] shall be initialized and set to 0 for each sub-band. HighRssi\_counter[subband] shall count number of occurrences where interference has exceeded the RSSI threshold given by [Before 05497845] NRCELL/tmpParam18 [05497845] NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/RssiThresholdForFastMute [End 05497845]. HighRssi\_subband shall be initialized and set to 0. HighRssi\_subband shall count number of subbands impacted by high interference.

During each RI monitoring window, per each RI comparison, If the RSSI in InitUL shall exceeds the RSSI threshold, the HighRssi\_counter[subband] shall be increment with 1.

gNB-DU shall perform the comparison in the time interval between the special slot and the previous special slot.

In parallel, gNB-DU shall calculate number of performed High RSSI comparison (numOfHRssiComparison). Those shorter consecutive UL slots of patterns shall be excluded from comparison scope. The numOfHRssiComparison is same to all subbands during each monitoring window.

At the end of each RI monitoring window, gNB-DU shall calculate HighRssiSlotRatio per subband (HighRssiSlotRatio[subband]) indicating the ratio of high RSSI impacted slots to the number of compared slots,

i.e. HighRssiSlotRatio [subband] = HighRssi\_counter[subband] / numOfHRssiComparison

If HighRssiSlotRatio[subband] exceeds NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/NrRiThresDurationRatio, then High RSSI occurs in the subband. The number of occurrences subband shall be counted to HighRSSI\_subband.

* If rdRiMonitorAllSsb="1" (see [11163711: rdRiMonitorAllSsb](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_GcSlgPvNEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU shall repeat above comparison processing for each SSB beam and get the result for each SSB beam, i.e. HighRSSI\_subband[SSB ID]
* If any HighRSSI\_subband[SSB ID] > 0,  gNB-DU shall determine High RSSI appears in current cell.
* Else if all HighRSSI\_subband [SSB ID] == 0,  gNB-DU shall determine High RSSI disappears in current cell.
* else if rdRiMonitorAllSsb="0", then
* If HighRSSI\_subband > 0,   gNB-DU shall determine High RSSI appears in current cell, i.e. HighRSSI\_initUL=true.
* Else if HighRSSI\_subband == 0, gNB-DU shall confirm HighRSSI\_initUL=false.

---

#### 3.21.2.3.0-6 Processing of RI measurement data RI state report via fault or CM parameter (ID: 11161764)

**3.21.2.3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11161768`)

Processing of RI measurement data
If NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/riStateReport is configured to 0, gNB-DU shall disable RI state reporting via fault-7525 or CM parameter NRCELL/[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO[End CB014133-A-UPD002]/riState.

Else if NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/riStateReport  is configured to 1, gNB-DU shall support to report RI state via CM parameter NRCELL/[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO[End CB014133-A-UPD002]/riState periodically, the reporting interval is equal to [Before CB014133-A-UPD002]rdRiUpdateInterval(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32375\_replaced([11163858](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktcdkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \* [End CB014133-A-UPD002]NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow.

Else if NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/riStateReport  is configured to 2, gNB-DU shall support to report RI state via fault-7525 periodically, the reporting interval is equal to [Before CB014133-A-UPD002]rdRiUpdateInterval \*[End CB014133-A-UPD002] NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow.

---

#### 3.21.2.3.0-7 Processing of RI measurement data RSSI measurement report via CM parameter (ID: 11161775)

**3.21.2.3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11161779`)

Processing of RI measurement data
If rdRiMonitorAllSsb="0" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31909\_replaced([11163711](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall disable RSSI measurements including worstRimRSSI, worstRimSsbId and worstRimSubbId on *initUL (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) reporting via corresponding CM parameters NRCELL/NRRIM\_INFO/worstRimRSSI, worstRimSsbId, and worstRimSubbId.*

Else if rdRiMonitorAllSsb="1" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31909\_replaced([11163711](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall support to report RSSI measurements on *initUL via corresponding CM parameters periodically in an interval of NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow.*

i.e.

* worstRimRSSI (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) via NRCELL/NRRIM\_INFO/worstRimRSSI
* worstRimSsbId (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) via NRCELL/NRRIM\_INFO/worstRimSsbId
* worstRimSubbId (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) via NRCELL/NRRIM\_INFO/worstRimSubbId

the reporting value is determined at the same moment of measurement report RI state determination (RI state1 as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or RI state2 as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9341\_replaced([11161641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 3.21.2.3.0-8 Processing of RI measurement data Determination of RI appearance in pilot window (ID: 12562998)

**3.21.2.3.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `12634415`)

Processing of RI measurement data
If NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/ actRiPilotDlMute =true, and NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMitigationManualTrigger = ‘disabled’, during RIM ”DL muting “ phase as result of 'Evaluation of conditional DL muting'(see [11161107: Evaluation of conditional DL muting](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), gNB-DU shall determine remote interference appearance in any sub-band as below procedure during each RI pilot window (see [12584508: Activation and Deactivation of RI pilot processing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Cs6ydDVBEfCKaNlcHOQWmg)) as below, otherwise gNB-DU shall deem no RI in pilot window.

gNB-DU shall perform the same comparison as [11161667: Determination of remote interference appearance](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8arWoPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) , including comparing the smoothed RI measurement results on 1st UL symbol after GP(InitUL) and 1st UL symbol each UL slot of each RI monitoring pattern with the RI threshold (see in [11161667: Determination of remote interference appearance](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8arWoPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and comparing RI level difference between two UL symbols in each slot of each RI monitoring pattern with the dropheight threshold (see [11161667: Determination of remote interference appearance](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8arWoPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In the beginning of RI pilot window, RIpilot\_counter[subband] [slot] shall be initialized and set to 0 and used to count number of patterns with RI occurrences for each subband and each slot during RI pilot window. RIpilotDetected\_subband shall be initialized and set to 0. RIpilotDetected\_subband shall count number of subbands impacted by remote interference during RI pilot window.

gNB-DU shall perform each time of RI comparison per subband traversing special slot and all consecutive UL slot[i] following the InitUL. gNB-DU shall determine the RI occurrence in RI pilot window using the same criteria as [11161667: Determination of remote interference appearance](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8arWoPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

During RI pilot window, gNB-DU shall count the number of RI occurrence for each subband and each slot ( RIpilot\_counter[subband] [slot] ) , and the number of RI pilot specific comparison (numOfRIPilotComparison) which is the same for all subbands.

gNB-DU shall use the same time interval between current RI occurrence pattern and the previous RI comparison pattern as [11161667: Determination of remote interference appearance](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8arWoPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

At the end of RI pilot window,

gNB-DU shall calculate RIpilotRatio[subband][slot] for each subband and each slot indicating the ratio of RIpilot\_counter[subband] [slot] to number of numOfRIpilotComparison, i.e. RIpilotSlotRatio[subband][slot] = RIpilot\_counter[subband] [slot] / numOfRIpilotComparison.

gNB-DU shall compare the RIpilotRatio[subband][slot] to the threshold NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/NrRiThresDurationRatio. If [PR867168] is equal to or [End PR867168]exceeds threshold, RI is confirmed detected in the subband, the RIpilotDetected\_subband shall be counted accordingly.

If RIpilotDetected\_subband > 0, gNB-DU shall confirm RI appearance in RI pilot window, else if *RIpilotDetected\_subband == 0 , gNB-DU shall confirm no RI in pilot window.*

---

#### 3.21.2.3.0-9 Processing of RI measurement data Determination of RI detection threshold (ID: 12713680)

**3.21.2.3.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `12738356`)

Processing of RI measurement data
If NRRIM\_PROFILE.actDynamicRiThresBaseCalc is equal to False, the RI detection threshold of all the subbands shall be determined by NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiThresBase (see [12744497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_dthjEH0AEfCiUemk-K-C4g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) in CPlane SFS).

else if NRRIM\_PROFILE.actDynamicRiThresBaseCalc is true,

> if NRRIMINFO.riThresBasePerSubband.riThresBaseSubband is null,  the RI detection threshold of subband X shall be determined by NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiThresBase.
>
> else the RI detection threshold of subband x shall be determined by NRRIMINFO.riThresBasePerSubband.riThresBaseSubband

where X is the subband index.

(see [12738571](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_bgeqYXjnEfCdZt6bzaG3fw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) in CPlane SFS)

---

#### 3.21.2.3.0-10 Processing of RI measurement data Maintain of RSSI data list for dynamic RI threshold (ID: 12738387)

**3.21.2.3.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `12738390`)

Processing of RI measurement data
gNB-DU shall maintain a list for each subband to track the RSSI data on the first uplink symbol after GP.

rssiOfFirstUlSymbol\_subband\_x[0,1,...,60]

where:

- x: indicates the subband index

- rssiOfFirstUlSymbol\_subband\_x[0]: indicates the number of occurrences of RSSI value which is equal to -60 dBm

- rssiOfFirstUlSymbol\_subband\_x[1]: indicates the number of occurrences of RSSI value which is equal to -61 dBm

- rssiOfFirstUlSymbol\_subband\_x[60]: indicates the number of occurrences of RSSI value which is equal to -120 dBm

If NRRIM\_PROFILE.actDynamicRiThresBaseCalc is true and NRCELL.actNrRim is not equal to '0:disabled' and RI state is equal to (0 or 1),  the RSSI value per SSB for subband x received at the end of each RI monitor window shall be rounded, and rssiOfFirstUlSymbol\_subband\_x shall be updated according to the rounded RSSI value. If the rounded RSSI value is larger than -60dBm or less than -120dBm, it shall be ignored.

All elements in rssiOfFirstUlSymbol\_subband\_x shall be set to 0 if any of below conditions is true:

* NRCELL.actNrRim is equal to "0:disabled"
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actDynamicRiThresBaseCalc is equal to False

---

#### 3.21.2.3.0-11 Processing of RI measurement data Dynamic RI threshold calculation and update (ID: 12738388)

**3.21.2.3.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `12738391`)

Processing of RI measurement data
12738391:
Processing of RI measurement data
If NRCELL.actNrRim is not equal to '0:disabled' and NRRIM\_PROFILE.actDynamicRiThresBaseCalc is equal to True, [Before CB014613-A-UPD001]an internal timer autoRiThresBaseCalcInterval defined by NRRIM\_PROFILE.autoRiThresBaseCalcInterval shall be started after the first RI monitor window. [CB014613-A-UPD001]

* if rdAutoRiThresBaseCalcInterval is equal to 0, the internal timer autoRiThresBaseCalcInterval defined by NRRIM\_PROFILE.autoRiThresBaseCalcInterval shall be started after the first RI monitor window.
* else, the internal timer autoRiThresBaseCalcInterval defined by rdAutoRiThresBaseCalcInterval (see [12780491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tBG6kI1WEfCrqOdGJPoCRA) ) shall be started after the first RI monitor window.

[End CB014613-A-UPD001]

When timer autoRiThresBaseCalcInterval expires, gNB-DU shall update the adjusted RI detection thresholds per subband as following:

* create the trimmed dataset according to rdRiDataTrimThreshold, which is the percentage of histogram entries to be trimmed from top and from bottom. rdRiDataTrimThreshold percentage of the highest and lowest values  in rssiOfFirstUlSymbol\_subband\_x(see 12738390) is trimmed.
* calculate the median (rssiMedian[subband\_index]) based on the trimmed rssiOfFirstUlSymbol\_subband\_x.

[CB014613-A-UPD001]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula for calculating the median of a grouped frequency distribution. The formula is written as:
Median = L + (n/2 - F) / f × w
Where:
\* L is the lower boundary of the median class
\* n is the total number of observations
\* F is the cumulative frequency of the class preceding the median class
\* f is the frequency of the median class
\* w is the width of the median class[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-09121448.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Where:

* L: lower boundary of the median bin
* n: total number of observations
* F: cumulative frequency before the median bin
* f: frequency of the median bin
* w: width of the median bin
* Note: w in our case is always 1.

[End CB014613-A-UPD001]

* calculate the Mean Absolute Deviation based on the trimmed rssiOfFirstUlSymbol\_subband\_x.

[Before CB014613-A-UPD001]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is:
$$ \frac{1}{N} \sum\_{i=1}^{N} |X\_i - \mu| $$
This expression represents the mean absolute deviation from the mean.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-08261534.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Where,

> N: the total number of trimmed RSSI samples
>
> Xi: a trimmed RSSI sample with value between -60dBm and -120dBm
>
> μ:  average of trimmed RSSI samples

[CB014613-A-UPD001]

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is for the Mean Absolute Deviation (MAD). It is written as:
MAD = $\frac{1}{n} \sum\_{i=1}^{k} f\_i \cdot |x\_i - \bar{x}|$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-09121451.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

Where:

* n: total number of data points (sum of frequencies)
* k: number of bins
* fi: frequency of bin i
* xi: midpoint of bin i
* [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical symbol, specifically the Greek letter chi ($\chi$) with a macron (a horizontal bar) above it. This symbol is often used in statistics to represent the sample mean. The image is a close-up of this symbol, with a slightly blurred effect.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-09121457.png[/image\_path][/image-3] : mean of the data (calculated with bin midpoints and frequencies)

[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a dark color on a white background. The formula is for calculating the mean of grouped data. It is represented as:
$\bar{x} = \frac{\Sigma(\text{midpoint} \times \text{frequency})}{\Sigma \text{frequency}}$
The formula uses the Greek letter Sigma ($\Sigma$) to denote summation. The numerator is the sum of the products of the midpoint and frequency for each group, and the denominator is the sum of the frequencies for all groups.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-09121456.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

[End CB014613-A-UPD001]

* Determine the adjusted RI detection threshold

nrThresBaseSubband[subband] = rssiMedian[subband] + NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiExpectedRssiRangeThres \* mad[subband],

Where, NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRiexpectedRssiRangeThres is the number of mean absolute deviations above the calculated mean to setup the threshold

* Inform the adjusted RI detection threshold to gNB-CU.
* update the RI detection threshold used by gNB-DU
* restart timer autoRiThresBaseCalcInterval

---

### 3.21.2.4 Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity

#### 3.21.2.4.0-1 Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity Processing of L1 pool RS detection capacity requesting (ID: 11161791)

**3.21.2.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11161803`)

Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity
11161803:
Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity
During RIM-RS detection processing (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13156\_replaced([11161857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall allocate available L1 RS detection capacity for this cell, as below

1) If gNB-DU is going to start RIM RS detection (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall allocate the available L1 RS detection capacity for this cell, as the result, the L1 RS detection capacity shall be available for usage in the incoming slow pooling window containing start boundary of RIM RS period (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13455\_replaced([11117569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- The RS detection command shall be set as “1”, indicating there is active RS detection in the cell.

**[Before CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- The RS detection request weight (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be set as “1”, indicating this is the first request of the incoming RS period, as there is starting boundary of RS period.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a timeline illustrating the request mode that an L2 RIM scheduler sends. The timeline is segmented into several blocks, each representing a part of a "BBRM period."
The text "The request mode which L2 RIM scheduler shall send" is positioned to the left of the timeline.
The timeline itself consists of the following segments:
1. **Ongoing request**: This is the first segment shown.
2. **First request Weight=1**: This segment follows the first "Ongoing request."
3. **Ongoing request Weight=2**: This segment follows "First request Weight=1." A vertical red line intersects this segment, indicating a specific point in time.
4. **Ongoing request**: This segment follows "Ongoing request Weight=2."
5. **Ongoing request**: This segment is the last one shown, following the previous "Ongoing request."
Above the first two segments, the text "One BBRM period" is displayed with a bracket encompassing these two segments, suggesting they constitute a single BBRM period.
Below the timeline, near the red vertical line, there are two lines of text:
\* "End point of preceding RS period"
\* "Start boundary of new RS period"
This indicates that the red line marks the transition between two RS (Request Scheduling or similar) periods.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11203.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

**[CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- If this is the first request of the incoming RS period, “new RS period” shall be marked as “true” indicating there is starting boundary of RS period during target pooling window.

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a timeline divided into several rectangular blocks, representing time periods or "pool windows." The blocks are colored black, yellow, and light green.
The leftmost block is black and labeled "request." Above this block, a bracket indicates "One pool window."
To the right of the black block is a yellow block labeled "Ongoing request."
Next to the "Ongoing request" block is a light green block labeled "First request."
To the right of the "First request" block are two more yellow blocks, which are empty.
Two curved blue arrows originate from the bottom of the "Ongoing request" and "First request" blocks and point downwards, with text below them reading "Allocation for usage in next pool window."
A vertical red line intersects the diagram between the "First request" block and the first empty yellow block. This red line has two labels pointing to it from the top right: "End of preceding RS period" and "Start boundary of new RS period."[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11203.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

**[End CB011127-A-UPD001]**

*Figure 1 The request mode which L2 RIM scheduler shall send.*

**[Before PR831007]**

- The minimum RS detection request shall be set as the L1 detection capacity requirement for **[Before CB011127-A-UPD001] revalidation detections (L1CapForRSrevalid, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24215\_replaced([11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** [CB011127-A-UPD001]  extra revalidation detections (L1CapForExtraRevalid, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24215\_replaced([11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) outside of RSDetectElements covered by Max capacity request **[End CB011127-A-UPD001] .**\*\*\*\*

**[PR831007]**

- The minimum RS detection request shall be set as the L1 detection capacity requirement for revalidation detections (L1CapForRSrevalid, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24215\_replaced([11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- The extra revalidation RS detection request shall be set as extra revalidation detections (L1CapForExtraRevalid, see [11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .

**[End PR831007]**

- The maximum RS detection request shall be set as sum of **[Before CB011127-A-UPD001] L1CapForRSrevalid+ L1CapForUnmeasure, where L1CapForUnmeasure can be** [CB011127-A-UPD001] L1CapForMaxRequest ,**[End CB011127-A-UPD001] seen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24217\_replaced([11161819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**\*\*\*\*

2) If the new RS detection process has set those “ongoing“ *RSDetectElements (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_ 13188) , in each slow pooling window within the same RS period, gNB-DU shall allocate the available L1 RS detection capacity for this cell using in the next slow pooling window (see figure 1).*

- The RS detection command shall be set as “1”, indicating there is active RS detection in the cell.

**[Before CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- The RS detection request weight (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be set as “2”, indicating this is the ongoing request during current RS period.

**[CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- “new RS period” shall be marked as “false” (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) indicating this is the ongoing request during current RS period.

**[End CB011127-A-UPD001]**

**[Before PR831007]**

- The minimum RS detection request shall be set as the L1 detection capacity requirement for**[Before CB011127-A-UPD001] revalidation detections (L1CapForRSrevalid, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24215\_replaced([11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** [CB011127-A-UPD001]  extra revalidation detections (L1CapForExtraRevalid, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24215\_replaced([11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) outside of RSDetectElements covered by Max capacity request **[End CB011127-A-UPD001] .**\*\*\*\*

- The maximum RS detection request shall be set as sum of **[Before CB011127-A-UPD001] L1CapForRSrevalid+L1CapForOngoing, where L1CapForOngoing can be seen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24219\_replaced([11161831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**[CB011127-A-UPD001] L1CapForMaxRequest (in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24217\_replaced([11161819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**[End CB011127-A-UPD001]**\*\*\*\*

**[PR831007]**

- The minimum RS detection request shall be set as the L1 detection capacity requirement for revalidation detections (L1CapForRSrevalid, see [11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- The extra revalidation RS detection request shall be set as extra revalidation detections (L1CapForExtraRevalid, see [11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .

- The maximum RS detection request shall be set as L1CapForOngoing (L1CapForExtraRevalid, see [11161831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**[End PR831007]**

3) If gNB-DU is going to stop new RIM RS detection but keep RIM RS revalidation, gNB-DU shall allocate available L1 RS detection capacity in the preceding slow pooling window for this cell to use in the next slow pooling window .

- The RS detection command shall be set as “1”, indicating there is active RS detection in the cell.

**[Before CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- The RS detection request weight (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be set as “0”, indicating this is no new RS detection during current RS period.

**[CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- “new RS period” shall be marked as “false” (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

**[End CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- The minimum RS detection request shall be set as the L1 detection capacity requirement for revalidation detections (L1CapForRSrevalid, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24215\_replaced([11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- The maximum RS detection request shall be set equal to the minimum RS detection request.

4) If gNB-DU is going to stop new RIM RS detection and revalidation RS detection, gNB-DU shall stop allocating RS detection capacity in the preceding slow pooling window so that this cell can de-activate RS detection status (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24193\_replaced([11215191](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0uvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the next slow pooling window .

- The RS detection command shall be set as “0”, indicating there is no active RS detection in the cell.

**[CB011127-A-UPD001]**

5) gNB-DU shall indicate current RS detection status, including

* number of "measured" RS detection elements (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), i.e. detection-complete RS elements.
* number of those RS detection elements in normal UL slots (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) included to determine L1CapForMaxRequest , i.e. detection-waiting normal RS elements.
* number of those RS detection elements in special slot (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) included to determine L1CapForMaxRequest, i.e. detection-waiting special RS elements.

**[End CB011127-A-UPD001]**

#### 3.21.2.4.0-2 Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity Calculate L1 detection capacity requirement for revalidation (ID: 11161808)

**3.21.2.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11161814`)

Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity
If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = true,  for the incoming slow pooling window  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ,

gNB-DU shall calculate the L1 detection capacity requirement for revalidation detection by aggregating total detection cost of all incoming revalidation detections in all UL-to-DL switching periods within the target slow pooling window .

The calculation result shall be the requirement of L1 RS detection capacity for the revalidation RS detection in the slow pooling window , L1CapForRSrevalid.

[CB011127-A-UPD001] gNB-DU shall also calculate the L1 detection capacity requirement for revalidation detection outside of those RSDetectElements which have been included into capacity requirement calculation of "L1CapForMaxRequest" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24217\_replaced([11161819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and "L1CapForOngoing" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24219\_replaced([11161831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), i.e. L1CapForExtraRevalid [END CB011127-A-UPD001]

---

#### 3.21.2.4.0-3 Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity Calculate L1 detection capacity requirement of the “first” request (ID: 11161819)

**3.21.2.4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11161824`)

Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity
If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = true,  for the incoming BBRM slow pooling window (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which contains start boundary of RS period, gNB-DU shall calculate the L1 detection capacity requirement for “first” new RS detection (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24213\_replaced([11161791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) by aggregating total detection cost of those RSDetectElements which locate in RSNewDetectRegion detections [CB011127-A-UPD001] ,within up to 2x frequency candidates (FC) ,  [END CB011127-A-UPD001] and are about to become “unmeasured” at the beginning of RIM RS period  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

The calculation result shall be the requirement of L1 RS detection capacity for the “first” new RS detection in the slow pooling window , L1CapForMaxRequest.

---

#### 3.21.2.4.0-4 Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity Calculate L1 detection capacity requirement of the “ongoing” request (ID: 11161831)

**3.21.2.4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11161836`)

Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity
If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling= true,  for the incoming slow pooling window (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) during the current RS period, gNB-DU shall calculate the L1 detection capacity requirement for “ongoing” new RS detection by aggregating total detection cost of all “ongoing” RSDetectElements during RSNewDetectRegiondetections (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the target slow pooling window.

The calculation result shall be the requirement of L1 RS detection capacity for the “ongoing” new RS detection in the BBRM slow pooling window ( L1CapForOngoing).

---

#### 3.21.2.4.0-5 Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity allocation L1 detection capacity for current cell (ID: 11161843)

**3.21.2.4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11161848`)

Request of L1 pooling RS detection capacity
If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = true, gNB-DU shall allocate L1 RS detection capacity (allocL1RsCap , see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24202\_replaced([11215255](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) to be used for RS detection in current cell during next slow pooling window  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

---

### 3.21.2.5 RIM RS detection

#### 3.21.2.5.0-1 RIM RS detection RIM-RS detection processing (ID: 11161857)

**3.21.2.5.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `13469824`)

RIM RS detection
13469824:
RIM RS detection
If actNrRim is configured to 3-“framework-0” OR 4-“framework-1”, gNB-DU shall start RIM-RS detecting processing [Before CB015735-A]as soon as gNB-DU enter RI state2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .[CB015735-A] if any of below condition is true,
\* as soon as gNB-DU enter RI state2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
\* NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect is True.
[End CB015735-A]
 
gNB-DU shall partition frequency and time resource in the UL duration of each TDD pattern into multiple RIM RS detection elements (RSDetectElement) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
 
gNB-DU shall allocate L1 RS detection capacity for this cell (i.e. *allocL1RsCap , see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24213\_replaced([11161791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in a period of the slow pooling window (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  If* allocL1RsCap >0 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24294\_replaced([11161843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), *allocL1RsCap shall be used for below RS detecting during the incoming period of the slow pooling window.* *then perform RS detecting as below:****\*
gNB-DU shall determine activation of new RIM RS detection* \*(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24355\_replaced([11162093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-DPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) before the beginning of each RIM RS period [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of the letters "P" and "E" in a stylized font. The letters appear to be made of a material that reflects light, creating a gradient of colors from yellow to blue. The background is white with a soft, blurred shadow effect around the edges.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11217.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13455\_replaced([11117569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**
 
following steps shall be used for RIM-RS type1 and RIM-RS type2 respectively
 
At the beginning of each RIM RS period [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of the letters "P" and "E" in a stylized font. The letters appear to be made of a material that reflects light, creating a gradient of colors from yellow to blue. The background is white with a soft, blurred shadow effect around the edges.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11217.001.png[/image\_path][/image-1] (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12626\_replaced([11117421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),
gNB-DU shall determine the range of *RSDetectElement for new RS detection (*RSNewDetectRegion) for each TDD pattern (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**During U-D switching period
gNB-DU shall firstly determine those RSDetectElements required for RIM-RS** revalidation (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15475\_replaced([11162234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .**gNB-DU shall calculate L1 Capacity for new RS detection (*L1CapacityNewDetection) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*
Then gNB-DU shall schedule new RS detection on the *RSNewDetectRegion based on L1CapacityNewDetection (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*
If gNB-DU didn't allocate enough L1 RS detection capacity (*allocL1RsCap, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24294\_replaced([11161843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) for this cell to fit new RS detection in current U-D switching period, then there is loss of RIM-RS detecting and detected result.*
During each Sslot or UL slot
gNB-DU shall check for those new revalidations from late L1H feedback and planned to be scheduled and calculate their detection cost (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15475\_replaced([11162234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
gNB-DU shall recalculate *L1CapacityNewDetection by subtracting detection cost of those scheduled new revalidations (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*

Upon the RIM-RS detecting report from 5G-L1-UL with available record, gNB-DU shall calculate detected setID (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13125\_replaced([11110087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpACd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
 
If *Nrcell-actNrRim is 4:framework-1 , gNB-DU shall determine "Enough" or "NotEnough" of RIM-RS type1 for the detected setID (see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_24844\_replaced([11162999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*
 
gNB-DU shall keep revalidation RIM-RS detection requesting for detected setID list (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ,** until following conditions**- stop it immediately if NRCell-*actNrRim is NOT 3-“framework-0” and NOT 4-“framework-1”,*
- OR stop it immediately when detected setID list becomes empty (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200\_replaced([11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
o Stop revalidation RIM-RS detection for RS type1 if detected set ID list of RS type1 becomes empty
o Stop revalidation RIM-RS detection for RS type2 if detected set ID list of RS type2 becomes empty
- OR RI state2 exits (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
 
gNB-DU shall keep RIM-RS new detection requesting until following conditions.
- stop it immediately if NRCell-*actNrRim is NOT 3-“framework-0” and NOT 4-“framework-1”,*
- OR [CB015735-A] if NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect=false , then [End CB015735-A] stop it immediately when RI state2 exits (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
- Or stop it by determining activation of new RIM RS detection (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24355\_replaced([11162093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-DPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

#### 3.21.2.5.0-2 RIM RS detection UL data reception for RIM-RS detection in eCPRI (ID: 11162029)

**3.21.2.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11162034`)

RIM RS detection
In case of eCPRI, for RIM-RS detection request (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13156\_replaced([11161857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),  5G-L2-PS shall schedule reception of UL data for each RIM-RS detection region carrying multiple RIM-RS detection requests for revalidation or new detection with below configurations:

- sharing receptions of PUSCH region [CB006991-C-UPD006] and scheduled ap-SRS (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16799\_replaced([11161550](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhyvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PRB range of aperiodic SRS)[End CB006991-C-UPD006],

- the UL symbol of special slot where pSRS is present shall be handled as scheduled region for RIM-RS detection.

- raising dedicated reception for unscheduled part.

[CB006991-C-UPD002]

- indicating the blank PRB parts within PRB range of RIM-RS detection region but outside of available PUSCH PRB region as below

o excluding PRACH region

o excluding dedicated long PUCCH resource and common long PUCCH resource

o considering expanding into pCSI PRBs area of PUCCH when /NRBTS/NRCELL.actDynUlResAlloc='true' (see in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[END CB006991-C-UPD002]

[PR697859]

5G-L2-PS shall stop requesting the RIM-RS detections on the entire slot if any unscheduled region inside this slot cannot be indicated.

[END PR697859]

[CB006991-C-UPD003]

5G-L2-PS shall stop requesting the RIM-RS detection if the number of blank PRB of one RIM-RS detection request is larger or equal to rdRimRsBlankPrbThres \* [RIM\_PROFILE- numRbForRs /48], where, rdRimRsBlankPrbThres (5G\_UP\_ALG\_16849\_replaced([11163837](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktb2kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall NOT be equal or higher than RIM\_PROFILE- numRbForRs.

[END CB006991-C-UPD003]

5G-L2-PS shall also indicate below configurations of UL data reception for each RIM-RS detecting region:

- pattern ID of beamweight in case of beamforming (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13190\_replaced([11162584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- index of spatial streams (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13206\_replaced([11162604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- the index of primary subcell.

#### 3.21.2.5.0-3 RIM RS detection Disabling periodic SRS and UL SU-MIMO based functions for RIM RS detection (ID: 11162042)

**3.21.2.5.0-3.0-9**  (ID: `13479898`)

RIM RS detection
gNB-DU shall trigger to disable pSRS based functionalities immediately during RIM RS detection according to following conditions

-  If NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim = 3 (framework-0) OR If NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim = "4:framework-1"

-  and  if gNB-DU start activation of new RIM RS detection (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24355\_replaced([11162093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-DPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

* and If gNB-DU had fetched available L1 detected resource capacity  (i.e. L1Capacity >0)  according to 5G\_UP\_5450\_replaced([11399506](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ugBFuPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

gNB-DU shall disable pSRS based functionalities as below:

- stop request pSRS reports for beam management (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2151\_replaced([11154219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrolPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6978\_replaced([11155803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

- stop request pSRS reports for UL SU-MIMO, and the evaluation of the required SINR shall depend on the SINR from PUSCH reception report independently (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11068\_replaced([11131303](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCz_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ,and this action shall invalidate simultaneous the mitigation of discarding pSRS UL SU MIMO (see 5G\_UPALG\_9459) in RI state2.

-  [Before CB007880-C-UPD001]stop request pSRS reports for positioning (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27490\_replaced([11158012](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_KlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in NRCELL [CB007880-C-UPD001] still request pSRS reports for positioning (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27490\_replaced([11158012](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_KlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in NRCELL as pSRS for positioning is a different EO(Executive Object) from RIM detection. Note that in this case L2PS will not fill any value for the measurement which is unreliable during RIM detection. Please note that in this case measurment abort might be triggered. [End CB007880-C-UPD001]

gNB-DU shall recover pSRS based functionalities above immediately in following conditions

* If (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is set to 0 or 1 )
* OR RI state2 exits (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* OR  If no RIM-RS detection and revalidation request in UL-DL switching period (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15475\_replaced([11162234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

-OR If gNB-DU gets no L1 detected resource capacity  (L1Capacity <=0)  according to 5G\_UP\_5450\_replaced([11399506](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ugBFuPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* OR if gNB-DU stop activation of new RIM RS detection (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24355\_replaced([11162093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-DPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  at the beginning of P\_t (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12626\_replaced([11117421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

If NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is switched from "4:framework-1" to "2:RI detection and mitigation",  or if fast muting SRS beam is activated (NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-fastMuteSrsBeamForRi= true), gNB-DU shall stop disabling pSRS based functionalities and switch to UL mitigation scheme according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9172\_replaced([11163373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 3.21.2.5.0-4 RIM RS detection Determination of activation of new RIM RS detection (ID: 11162093)

**3.21.2.5.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `13479148`)

RIM RS detection
during RIM RS detection processing (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13156\_replaced([11161857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall determine if new RIM RS detection processing shall be activated.

- gNB-DU shall start new RIM RS detection processing (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in following cases at the beginning of P\_t

o gNB-DU shall allocate available L1 RS detection resources capacity for this cell scheduler, i.e.*allocL1RsCap >0 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24294\_replaced([11161843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .*

o And

 If *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsDetectionWindow  is not "0: disable RS detection"*

 And when RI is detected (2a=true) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB015735-A]or NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect is true.[End CB015735-A]

- gNB-DU shall stop new RIM RS detection processing (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at the beginning of P\_t (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12626\_replaced([11117421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in following cases

o If no L1 detected resources capacity  ( i.e.*allocL1RsCap =0,see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24294\_replaced([11161843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is allocated for   this cell scheduler to perform new RIM RS detection (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*

o OR

 If *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsDetectionWindow = 0: disable RS detection;*

 Or, If *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsDetectionWindow is not "0: disable RS detection"*

 And when RI is not detected (2a=false) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB015735-A] AND NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect is False.[End CB015735-A]

At the beginning of RIM RS P\_t (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13455\_replaced([11117569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  ,
gNB-DU shall set those RSDetectElements with  status(“ongoing” ) to status("measured").
gNB-DU shall determine the range of *RSDetectElements for new RS detection (*RSNewDetectRegion) for each TDD pattern by** If *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsDetectionWindow=”1:sloping base” including those *RSDetectElements containing those UL symbols from min (*EndULsymbol, *RIEndSymbol+* \*x ( from BIx y)) to the DistanceThresholdSymbol,******where* EndULSymbol is the last UL symbol the TDD pattern, \*RIEndSymbol is in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9651\_replaced([11161729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), DistanceThresholdSymbol is the NRCELL/NRRIM\_profile/rsDistanceThreshold UL symbol after Guard symbols**
 Else If *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsDetectionWindow=” 2:special+UL slots” ,*
 - For NEAR repetitions, *RSDetectElements containing those UL symbols in special slot and the following first UL slot except UL symbols from initUL to DistanceThresholdSymbol,*
 - For FAR repetitions,
  > if *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rsNearFarConfig is "1:near-far config1",*
   >>*RSDetectElements containing those UL symbols inside special slot and the following first UL slot except UL symbols from initUL to max(0, DistanceThresholdSymbol - x (from from BIx y)).*
  > if *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rsNearFarConfig is "2:near-far config2",*
   >>*RSDetectElements containing those UL symbols inside special slot and the following first UL slot except UL symbols from initUL to max(0, DistanceThresholdSymbol - 14 - x  (from from BIx y)).*
 Else If *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsDetectionWindow=” 3:special+2UL slots” ,*
 - For NEAR repetitions, *RSDetectElements containing those UL symbols in special slot and the following first and second UL slot except UL symbols from initUL to DistanceThresholdSymbol,*
 - For FAR repetitions,
  > if *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rsNearFarConfig is "1:near-far config1",*
   >>*RSDetectElements containing those UL symbols inside special slot and the following first and second UL slot except UL symbols from initUL to max(0, DistanceThresholdSymbol - x (from from BIx y)).*
  > if *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rsNearFarConfig is "2:near-far config2",*
   >>*RSDetectElements containing those UL symbols inside special slot and the following first and second UL slot except UL symbols from initUL to max(0, DistanceThresholdSymbol - 14 - x  (from from BIx y)).*
 
When all RSDetectElements among RSNewDetectRegion have NoT “unmeasured” status, all the RSDetectElements in TDD pattern shall be changed to status(”unmeasured”).
 
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = false, Among RSNewDetectRegion, gNB-DU shall traverse those RSDetectElements during *RSNewDetectRegion and determine the element list for new RS detection (*newDetectElementlist) as below steps:**1. Set the remaining L1 capacity  (L1RemainingCapacity) equal to the RS detection capacity for current cell that was allocated by gNB (*allocL1RsCap, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24294\_replaced([11161843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*2. [CB015735-A]If NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect is True, travering all unmeasured RSDetectElements with descending index from the highest index in the RSNewDetectRegion. Else, [End CB015735-A]Traversing all unmeasured RSDetectElements with ascending index from the lowest index in the RSNewDetectRegion,
  > if the detection cost of RSDetectElement[i] fit the remaining L1 Capacity, then
   >>  if the status of the RSDetectElement is “unmeasured” and if its detection cost <=  L1RemainingCapacity, the RSDetectElement shall be set as status("ongoing"), then calculate L1RemainingCapacity by subtracting total capacity cost (in unit of numOfSequences \* numOfSymbols) from current remaining L1 capacity.
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = true, among RSNewDetectRegion, gNB-DU shall traverse those RSDetectElements during* RSNewDetectRegion and determine the element list for new RS detection (*newDetectElementlist) as below steps:**1. Set the remaining L1 capacity (L1RemainingCapacity)**equal to the RS detection capacity for current cell that was allocated by gNB (*allocL1RsCap, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24294\_replaced([11161843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***
 2. [CB015735-A]If NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect is True, travering all unmeasured RSDetectElements with descending index from the highest index in the RSNewDetectRegion. Else, [End CB015735-A]traversing all unmeasured RSDetectElements with ascending index from the lowest index in the RSNewDetectRegion,
  > if the detection cost of RSDetectElement[i] fit the remaining L1 Capacity, then loop the fitted RSDetectElement[i] and those RSDetectElements with same FC index to the RSDetectElement[i] in ascending RSDetectElement index.
   >> if the status of the RSDetectElement is “unmeasured” and if its detection cost <= L1RemainingCapacity, the RSDetectElement shall be set as status("ongoing"), then calculate L1RemainingCapacity by subtracting total capacity cost (in unit of numOfSequences \* numOfSymbols) from current remaining L1 capacity.
 3. Do step 2 again, then stop traversing.
During U-D switching period  [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "γt RIM". The text is blurry and appears to be in a sans-serif font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, purple, and orange.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11237.002.png[/image\_path][/image-2]
gNB-DU shall calculate available L1 Capacity for new RS detection (L1CapacityNewDetection) by subtracting total detection cost of all revalidations scheduled in current U-D switching period (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15475\_replaced([11162234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from the current L1 remaining Capacity.
 During each Sslot or UL slot
gNB-DU shall update L1CapacityNewDetection by subtracting detection cost of those scheduled new revalidations. (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15475\_replaced([11162234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
**If *NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsDetectionWindow is NOT ”1:sloping base” , *nearFarShift =0; else, gNB-DU shall calculate* nearFarShift based on \*NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsNearFarConfig by:*****nearFarShift =0 for “near” occasion of U-D periodnearFarShift = floor(([image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: `max(x, 7) + (rsNearFarConfig - 1) * 14`. The text is slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11237.003.png[/image\_path][/image-3])\*/7) \*\* numOfFC (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for “far” occasion of U-D period***[CB015735-A]If NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRsContinuousDetect is True, those RSDetectElements belonging to current slot by descending element index(i\_element). Else, [End CB015735-A]Traversing those RSDetectElements belonging to current slot by ascending element index(i\_element), when i\_element >= nearFarShift , if its corresponding RSDetectElement(i\_element - nearFarShift) has status(“ongoing”), gNB-DU shall schedule the RSDetectElement(i\_element) for new RS detection as following processing:
if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = False,
1. If the RSDetectElement need to be dropped according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16851\_replaced([11162029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), those expected and skipped new detections of RSDetectElements shall be respectively counted.
2. Else, those expected new detections of RSDetectElements shall be respectively counted.
 
 
if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = True(5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RIM-RS monitoring PRBs from the unscheduled PRB regions, if any, can be used only if there are still sufficient PRBs left from the total usable PRBs available in the current slot for the PUSCH area and this limit is not going to be exceeded(5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
1. For each frequency candidate with ascending index,
a. If any RSDetectElement belongs to this frequency candidate, and if the RSDetectElement with blank PRB exceed threshold (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16851\_replaced([11162029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), skip step b.
b. For each RSDetectElement belonging to current slot,
i. If scheduleAllowedRSDetectElement (k) is true, where k is the index of this RSDetectElement, skip step ii.
ii. If the frequency resource of this RSDetectElement is same as this frequency candidate,
1. If scheduleAllowedFrequencyCandidate(i) is true, set scheduleAllowedRSDetectElement (k) to true. Skip step 2.
2. calculate the total number of unique PRBs that belongs to this RSDetectElement but they are not used by any other channel/signal on current slot and assign to amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i), where i is the index of this frequency candidate. If amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i) fit the remaining PRB, set  scheduleAllowedFrequencyCandidate(i)  to true, and set scheduleAllowedRSDetectElement (k) to true, and update prbRemainingCapacity = prbRemainingCapacity - amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i).
2. calculate the total number of unique PRBs per symbol* *that belongs to this RSDetectElement but they are not used by any other channel/signal on current slot and assign to amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i,j), where i is the index of this frequency candidate**, j is the index of symbol. If all amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i,j) in current slot* *fit the remaining PRB, set  scheduleAllowedFrequencyCandidate(i)  to true, and set scheduleAllowedRSDetectElement (k) to true, and update prbRemainingCapacity = prbRemainingCapacity - amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i)* *prbRemainingCapacity[j] = prbRemainingCapacity[j] - amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i,j).****\****
 
2. For each RSDetectElement belonging to current slot,
a. If scheduleAllowedRSDetectElement[k] is true, this RSDetectElement shall be scheduled. Those expected new detection of RSDetectElements shall be respectively counted.
b. Else,
i. This RSDetectElement shall be skipped.
ii. If PUSCH is no longer overlapping with RIM-RS, the original beam weight shall be recovered (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13190\_replaced([11162584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
iii. If SRS is no longer overlapping with RIM-RS, the full sector beam shall still be used (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13190\_replaced([11162584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
iv. Those expected and skipped new detection of RSDetectElements shall be respectively counted
gNB-DU shall calculate its practical detection cost by subtracting cost of all revalidation detections scheduled in the same RSDetectElement  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15475\_replaced([11162234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
gNB-DU shall determine *newDetectionSequence list* by excluding those N\_scids scheduled for revalidation in current *RSDetectElement (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15475\_replaced([11162234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from the RS sequence list given by* NRRIM\_PROFILE/rsType1NScId.***\*
gNB-DU shall calculate number of available sequence,* n\_seq = min(floor(remaining L1CapacityNewDetection / *numOfSymbol) , sizeOf (*newDetectionSequence)),**\*
where

> *numOfSymbol is 7 for UL slot and* y for special slot BIx y (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))***numOfSequence is from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),*
> then gNB-DU shall schedule upto *n\_seq preceding index of RS sequences from* newDetectionSequence list and schedule them for new RS detection on all symbols in the RSDetectElement.**
> gNB-DU shall update the remaining L1CapacityNewDetection by subtracting total detection cost of scheduled available sequences in the RSDetectElement from the previous remaining L1CapacityNewDetection.

During each S-slot or UL slot:

gNB-DU shall check those new revalidations that would be planned due to 5G-L1-UL late response feedback and calculate their detection cost.

if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = False,

1. If the RSDetectElement need to be dropped according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16851\_replaced([11162029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), those expected and skipped revalidation of RSDetectElements shall be respectively counted.

2. Else, those expected revalidation of RSDetectElements shall be respectively counted.

if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = True (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RIM-RS monitoring PRBs from the unscheduled PRB regions, if any, can be used only if there are still sufficient PRBs left from the total usable PRBs available in the current slot for the PUSCH area and this limit is not going to be exceeded(5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

1. Calculate the remaining PRB resource for unscheduled regions per symbol, set prbRemainingCapacity[j] = availableUlPrb (the available amount of PRBs for PUSCH in current slot, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) – (the amount of PRBs allocated to PUSCH/apSRS on symbol j in current slot), where j is the index of OFDM symbols.

2. For each RSDetectElement belonging to current slot, set scheduleAllowedRSDetectElement(k) to false to indicate RSDetectElement with index k is not allowed to be scheduled in the current slot.

3. For each frequency candidate, set scheduleAllowedFrequencyCandidate(i) to fasle to indicate the frequency candidate with index i is not allowed to be scheduled in the current slot.

4. For each frequency candidate with ascending index,

a. If any RSDetectElement belongs to this frequency candidate, and if the RSDetectElement with blank PRB exceed threshold (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16851\_replaced([11162029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), skip step b.

b. For each RSDetectElement belonging to current slot,

i. If the frequency resource of this RSDetectElement is same as this frequency candidate,

1. If scheduleAllowedFrequencyCandidate(i) is true, set scheduleAllowedRSDetectElement (k) to true. Skip step 2.

2.   calculate the total number of unique PRBs per symbol that belongs to this RSDetectElement but they are not used by any other channel/signal on current slot and assign to amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i,j), where i is the index of this frequency candidate, j is the index of symbo If all amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i,j) in current slot fit the remaining PRB, set  scheduleAllowedFrequencyCandidate(i)  to true, and set scheduleAllowedRSDetectElement (k) to true, and update  prbRemainingCapacity[j] = prbRemainingCapacity[j] - amountPrbUnscheduledRegion(i,j).

5. For each RSDetectElement belonging to current slot,

a. If scheduleAllowedRSDetectElement[k] is true, this RSDetectElement shall be scheduled. Those expected revalidation of RSDetectElements shall be respectively counted.

b. Else,

i. This RSDetectElement shall be skipped.

ii. If PUSCH is no longer overlapping with RIM-RS, the original beam weight shall be recovered (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13190\_replaced([11162584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

iii. If SRS is no longer overlapping with RIM-RS, the full sector beam shall still be used (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13190\_replaced([11162584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

iv. Those expected and skipped revalidation of RSDetectElements shall be respectively counted.

gNB-DU shall calculate detection cost of those new revalidation within those RSDetectElements with blank PRB exceeding threshold.

gNB-DU shall recalculate L1CapacityNewDetection by subtracting those detection cost of available revalidation RSDetectElements. (see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The detection cost of revalidation shall be calculated as the number of symbol candidates within UL duration in the U-D period [image-27][image\_desc]The image contains the text "γt RIM". The text is blurry and appears to be in a sans-serif font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, purple, and orange. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11241.009.png[/image\_path][/image-27] .

The revalidation cost of RSDetectElement shall be total detection cost of all revalidation requests contained by the RSDetectElement.

Total revalidation cost shall be calculated among all RSDetectElements containing revalidation requests in the U-D period [image-28][image\_desc]The image contains the text "γt RIM". The text is blurry and appears to be in a sans-serif font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, purple, and orange. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11241.009.png[/image\_path][/image-28]

#### 3.21.2.5.0-7 RIM RS detection Configuration of beamweight for RIM RS detecting (ID: 11162584)

**3.21.2.5.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11162598`)

RIM RS detection
if NRBTS/NRCELL-actBeamforming = true, 5G-L2-PS shall use the single full-sector beam (see the definition of the single full-sector beam in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1933\_replaced([11111686](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpPTD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2037\_replaced([11112372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The beam weight used for RIM-RS is configured by C-Plane in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2480\_replaced([11288965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8fvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2483\_replaced([11289095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-xBfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as the beam weight of RIM RS reception (RIMRSbeam) when there is no other scheduling sharing RIM RS detection element  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and spatial streams (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13206\_replaced([11162604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in primary subcell .

If there are UEs scheudled with overlapping part to RIM RS detection element, same pattern ID of beamweight shall be used for the beam of channel grants and the reception beam of RIM RS in the same spatial streams:

* PUSCH grant shall use the RIM RS beam
* apSRS shall use the RIM RS beam
* UL symbol in special slot which can be configured for pSRS shall use the RIM RS beam

taking C4 subcell as below example, when following cases take place in the stream{2,3} where RIM RS reception is scheduled

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| With overlapping with RIM RS region |  | Spatial streams w/o RIM RS | Spatial Stream w/ RIM RS |
|  | PUSCH | No change | RIM RS beam |
|  | AP-SRS for SU-MIMO | No change | RIM RS beam |
|  | p-SRS for SU-MIMO | no change | RIM RS beam |
|  |  |  |  |

where Spatial Stream w/ RIM RS is given in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13206\_replaced([11162604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CNI-95601]

If RIM-RS detection element scheudling in a slot is skipped (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15475\_replaced([11162234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

- If PUSCH is no longer overlapping with RIM-RS, the original beam weight shall be recovered.

- If SRS is no longer overlapping with RIM-RS, the full sector beam shall still be used.

[End CNI-95601]

#### 3.21.2.5.0-8 RIM RS detection Configuration of spatial stream for RIM RS detecting (ID: 11162604)

**3.21.2.5.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11162615`)

RIM RS detection
In primary subcell (Cn), 5G-L2-PS shall allocate lastest 2 streams related resource for RIM RS detecting as below:

· numStreamIndex = 2

· streamIndex = {n-2, n-1}

[CB010708-I]where, n is equal to NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming. [End CB010708-I]

#### 3.21.2.5.0-9 RIM RS detection RIM RS detection elements (ID: 11162620)

**3.21.2.5.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11162643`)

RIM RS detection
11162643:
RIM RS detection
5G-L2-PS shall partition frequency and time resource in the UL duration per UD-switching period into multiple RIM RS detection elements (RSDetectElement). Each element consists of [CB009823-F]

* If  NRBTS/NRCELL-actNrRim is configured to 3-“framework-0” ,  [End CB009823-F] RIM\_PROFILE- numRbForRs in frequency and a halfslot in time.

[CB009823-F] – else If  NRBTS/NRCELL-actNrRim is configured to 4-“framework-1” ,  [End CB009823-F] occupied PRB range in frequency and a halfslot in time.

Where halfslot means :

> symbol 0~6, or 7~13 For UL slot
>
> symbol (14-y)~13 for special slot BIx y (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB009823-F] And occupied PRB range means the consecutive complete PRB range which can cover the start frequency point and all following subcarriers of  RIM\_PROFILE- numRbForRs used for RIM RS transmission (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13075\_replaced([11118073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB009823-F]

All the elements in a TDD pattern shall be indexed firstly through frequency candidate (FC) list (given by RIM\_PROFILE- startRbForRs), and secondly through half slot from D-U switching point towards U-D switching point.

An example for RSDetectElements in the TDD pattern with 1xSslot+2xUL slots

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating a data structure related to a cellular network. The diagram is divided into two main sections: "No.x Cn subcell" and "No.1 Cn subcell". The "No.1 Cn subcell" section contains a table labeled "Stream {n-2,n-1}".
The table has two columns on the left: "RS DetectElement" and a column with numerical indices [3], [2], [1], [0]. The remaining columns are headers representing different streams: "S-Slot(4)", "UL 1.1 (3)", "UL 1.2 (2)", "UL 2.1 (1)", and "UL 2.2 (0)". The cells within the table contain numerical values.
Several annotations are present:
- An arrow points from the index of "half slot" to the header "UL 2.1 (1)".
- An arrow points from the index of "RSDetectElement" to the cell containing the value "5" in the row indexed [1] and column "UL 2.1 (1)".
- An arrow points from the index of "RIM\_PROFILE.startRbForRs" to the row indexed [0] under the "RS DetectElement" column.
- A bracket labeled "RSDetectElement" and "halfslot" points to the cell containing "5".
- A bracket labeled "RIM\_PROFILE.numRbForRss" is positioned to the right of the table.
The table can be represented as follows:

| RS DetectElement | S-Slot(4) | UL 1.1 (3) | UL 1.2 (2) | UL 2.1 (1) | UL 2.2 (0) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [3] | 19 | 15 | 11 | 7 | 3 |
| [2] | 18 | 14 | 10 | 6 | 2 |
| [1] | 17 | 13 | 9 | 5 | 1 |
| [0] | 16 | 12 | 8 | 4 | 0 |

An example for RSDetectElements in the TDD pattern with 1xSslot+1xUL slot

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a table with a header row and two data rows. The header row has four columns: "RS DetectElement", "S-Slot(2)", "UL 1.1 (1)", and "UL 1.2 (0)". The first column, "RS DetectElement", has two sub-rows labeled "[1]" and "[0]". The data rows contain numerical values corresponding to the column headers.

| [0] | 4 | 2 | 0 |

Each element shall store

- an enum state = {unmeasured, measured, ongoing}, where default is set as unmeasured

- measurement cost is numOfSequences \* numOfSymbols

where

> numOfSequence is number of sequence candidates(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12686\_replaced([11118096](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
>
> numOfSymbol is 7 for UL slot and y for special slot BIx y (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
