#### 3.21.2.5.0-11 RIM RS detection Determination of near-far configuration for detected RIM RS (ID: 11162888)

**3.21.2.5.0-11.0-2**  (ID: `11162993`)

RIM RS detection
11162993:
RIM RS detection
If Nrcell-actNrRim is 3:framework-0 [CB009823-B] OR  4:framework-1 [END CB009823-B] , upon each valid RIM RS detection report from 5G-L1-UL (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13132\_replaced([11110163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpAph_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , gNB-DU shall determine 'near' or 'far' configuration and calculate RS propragation distance in term of symbol numbers since guard period (RSSymbolDistanceSinceGP ) for the detected setID (see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13196\_replaced([11162649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
 
[CB009823-B] following steps shall be used for RIM-RS type1 and RIM-RS type2 respectively. [END CB009823-B]
 
If NRRIM\_PROFILE-rsNearFarConfig = 0-“near only”, all detected RIM RS are  “near” configuration
else If NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rsNearFarConfig = 1-“ near-far config1”  OR 2-“ near-far config2”,  based on [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "i, t, RIM". The text is blurry and appears to be in a digital font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, purple, and orange. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11256.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] calculation for each detected RIM-RS in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13196\_replaced([11162649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU shall determine its 'near' or 'far' configuration as below
- to calculate [image-1][image\_desc]$\gamma\_{t}^{\text{RIM}} = (t\_{r}^{\text{RIM}} - T\_{\text{start}}) \text{MOD } R\_{i}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11256.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
Where

> [image-2][image\_desc]The image is a close-up, blurry, and pixelated shot of the letters "R" and "i" with a faint "L" underneath the "i". The letters are in a gradient of colors, with shades of blue, orange, and yellow. #### 3.21.2.5.0-12 RIM RS detection Determination of Enough or NotEnough indication for detected RIM RS type1 (ID: 11162999)

**3.21.2.5.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11163026`)

RIM RS detection
11163026:
RIM RS detection
If Nrcell-actNrRim is 4:framework-1 , upon each valid RIM RS detection report including  [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a stylized font and appears to be a subscript followed by a larger expression.

$i\_5 \cdot RIM\_1$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11258.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] for RIM-RS type1 from rimrstriplet[j] in RIM RS detection report of DU  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13132\_replaced([11110163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpAph_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) corresponding to new RS detection request (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13188\_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall determine "Enough" or "NotEnough" of RIM-RS type1 for each RIM RS detection report from DU (see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13196\_replaced([11162649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- If  [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a stylized font and appears to be a subscript followed by a larger expression.

#### 3.21.2.5.0-13 RIM RS detection Determination of RIM RS detected (ID: 11163032)

**3.21.2.5.0-13.0-2**  (ID: `11163045`)

RIM RS detection
5G-L2-PS shall determine if RIM RS is detected or not upon the RIM RS detection report from 5G-L1-UL [CB009823-B] separately for RS type1 and type2 [END CB009823-B].

After gNB-DU calculated the detected setID as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13196\_replaced([11162649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU shall record it into detected set ID list if it satisfies filtering criteria (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13204\_replaced([11163050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If the “confirmed” record in detected set ID list  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13204\_replaced([11163050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) becomes NOT empty after updating, gNB-DU shall confirm RIM RS detected immediately.

[CB009823-B]

- If detected set ID list of RS type1 becomes NOT empty, RS1 detected (2b=true) shall be confirmed

- If detected set ID list of RS type2 becomes NOT empty, RS2 detected (2c=true) shall be confirmed [END CB009823-B]

Else If the “suspect” record in detected set ID list  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13204\_replaced([11163050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) exists, gNB-DU shall confirm RIM RS suspect.

Else if the record in detected set ID list becomes empty at the end of current RS transmission period, gNB-DU shall confirm RIM RS disappears.

[CB009823-B]

- If detected set ID list of RS type1 becomes empty, No RS1 detected (2b=false) shall be confirmed

- If detected set ID list of RS type2 becomes empty, No RS2 detected (2c=false) shall be confirmed

[END CB009823-B]

---

> N\_attempLoss is the number of detections attempts loss which shall be counted per RIM RS detection elements (see [11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_BB5ZYPvNEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) within one repetition window of  (see [11117616](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_O-tPUPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) due to

>> and any RS detection request drop caused by

>>>or, lack of available UL PRB resource in case of slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = true (see [11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_-nmhMPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

>>>Or, the number of blank PRB exceeding threshold (see [11162029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_-OW6wPvMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

N\_attempLoss shall be counted separately for "near" transmissions case and "far" transmissions case and separately used to compensate the detections attempts in near transmissions case and far transmissions case.

#### 3.21.2.5.0-15 RIM RS detection RIM-RS detection report via fault or CM parameter (ID: 11163356)

**3.21.2.5.0-15.0-1**  (ID: `11163362`)

RIM RS detection
If NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/rimRsStateReport is configured to 0, gNB-DU shall disable RIM-RS detection reporting via fault-7527 or CM parameter NRCELL/**[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO/setIdType1List**[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO/rimRsSetIdType1**[End CB014133-A-UPD002] or NRCELL/**[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO/setIdType2List**[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO/rimRsSetIdType2**[End CB014133-A-UPD002].***\******\***

Else if NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/rimRsStateReport is configured to 1,

- if NRRIM\_PROFILE/actNrRim=3, gNB-DU shall support to report RIM-RS detections via CM parameter NRCELL/**[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO/setIdType1List**[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO/rimRsSetIdType1**[End CB014133-A-UPD002] periodically, the reporting interval is equal to [Before CB014133-A-UPD003]rdRimRsUpdateInterval(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32376\_replaced([11163868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktcdk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \* RS-1 transmission period(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13070\_replaced([11117417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[CB014133-A-UPD003]NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow[End CB014133-A-UPD003].**\*\*\*\*

- else if NRRIM\_PROFILE/actNrRim=4, gNB-DU shall support to report RIM-RS detections via CM parameter NRCELL/**[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO/setIdType1List**[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO/rimRsSetIdType1**[End CB014133-A-UPD002] and NRCELL/**[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO/setIdType2List**[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO/rimRsSetIdType2**[End CB014133-A-UPD002] periodically, [CB014133-A-UPD003]which is equal to NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow.[End CB014133-A-UPD003]***\******\***

[Before CB014133-A-UPD003]

-- The first update of NRCELL/**[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO/setIdType1List**[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO/rimRsSetIdType1**[End CB014133-A-UPD002] is at the end of RS-1 transmission period with interval which equals to (rdRimRsUpdateInterval \* (RS-1 transmission period + RS-2 transmission period(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13070\_replaced([11117417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) - RS-2 transmission period), and the subsequent updates is at the end of RS-1 transmission period with interval which is equal to rdRimRsUpdateInterval \* (RS-1 transmission period + RS-2 transmission period) .**\*\*\*\*

-- NRCELL/**[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO/setIdType2List**[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO/rimRsSetIdType2**[End CB014133-A-UPD002] is updated at the end of RS-2 transmission period with interval which is equal to rdRimRsUpdateInterval \* (RS-1 transmission period + RS-2 transmission period).**\*\*\*\*

[End CB014133-A-UPD003]

Else if NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/rimRsStateReport is configured to 2, gNB-DU shall support to report RIM-RS detection via fault-7527 periodically, the reporting interval is equal to [Before CB014133-A-UPD003]rdRimRsUpdateInterval \* RS transmission period.[CB014133-A-UPD003]NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow.[End CB014133-A-UPD003]

The maximum number of setIds contained in NRCELL/**[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO/setIdType1List**[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO/rimRsSetIdType1**[End CB014133-A-UPD002] and NRCELL/**[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO/setIdType2List**[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO/rimRsSetIdType2**[End CB014133-A-UPD002] is defined by **[Before CB014133-B-UPD001]rdRimRsSetListLength (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32374\_replaced([11163848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktb2lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**[CB014133-B-UPD001]rimRsSetidListLength**[End CB014133-B-UPD001]. If the number of detected setIDs exceeds** [Before CB014133-B-UPD001]rdRimRsSetListLength**[CB014133-B-UPD001]rimRsSetidListLength**[End CB014133-B-UPD001], the detected setIDs shall be ranked according their power level in descending order, and the top **[Before CB014133-B-UPD001]rdRimRsSetListLength**[CB014133-B-UPD001]rimRsSetidListLength**[End CB014133-B-UPD001] setIDs shall be reported.*****\*******\*******\*******\****

### 3.21.2.6 UL Mitigation for remote interference

#### 3.21.2.6.0-1 UL Mitigation for remote interference Mitigation solution to remote interference detection (ID: 11163373)

**3.21.2.6.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11163397`)

UL Mitigation for remote interference
In case of remote interference appearance and mitigation mode is activated (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), or if fast muting SRS beam is activated when NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-fastMuteSrsBeamForRi= true AND highRSSI\_initUL=true (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31913\_replaced([11161754](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall take RI specific mitigations for SRS:

- stop request SRS reports for beam management (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2151\_replaced([11154219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrolPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6978\_replaced([11155803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if SRS symbol is allocated in special slot.

- discard SRS reports for SU-MIMO (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9459\_replaced([11163403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  if SRS symbol is allocated in special slot.

- [Before CB007880-C-UPD001][CB007880-C] discard SRS reports for positioning regarding UL-RTOA measurements and UL SRS-RSRP (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27490\_replaced([11158012](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_KlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if SRS symbol is allocated in special slot in NRCELL.[End CB007880-C] [End CB007880-C-UPD001]

In case of remote interference appearance and mitigation mode is activated (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall take below RI specific mitigations :

- enhance power configuration for random access (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9173\_replaced([11163434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

#### 3.21.2.6.0-2 UL Mitigation for remote interference Discard pSRS measurement for UL SU MIMO (ID: 11163403)

**3.21.2.6.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11163427`)

UL Mitigation for remote interference
In case of remote interference appearance and mitigation action is activated (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), or if fast muting SRS beam is activated when NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-fastMuteSrsBeamForRi= true AND highRSSI\_initUL=true (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31913\_replaced([11161754](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and if SRS symbol is allocated in special slot, the evaluation of the required SINR shall depend on PUSCH only, that is to use post SINR after equalization(5G\_UP\_ALG\_25392\_replaced([11131411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCp5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) independently (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3081\_replaced([11131259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Existing state machines apply (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3238\_replaced([11155604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3240\_replaced([11155613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with updated rule for remote interference case to discard SU\_MIMO report :

- if SRS is non DTX and sinrOfAnt[0]... sinrOfAnt[nbRx] from SRS are all equal or greater than rdSrsNonDtxMinPower (see 5G\_L2\_1428\_replaced([11186208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_274Hc_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , SU UL MIMO report from SRS shall be VALID

- otherwise (i.e. SRS is DTX or at least one sinrOfAnt[i] < rdSrsNonDtxMinPower ), SU UL MIMO report from SRS shall be DISCARDED.

[Before CB007880-C-UPD001][CB007880-C]

Existing state machines apply (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3238\_replaced([11155604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3240\_replaced([11155613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with updated rule for remote interference case to discard Positioning Measurement report as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27490\_replaced([11158012](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_KlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB007880-C]

[End CB007880-C-UPD001]

when remote interference disappears or mitigation mode is deactivated (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall recover SRS based functionalities and re-use SU UL MIMO report based on non-DTXed SRS measurement received from L1 layer  [Before CB007880-C-UPD001][CB007880-C] and Positioning Measurment report from SRS (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27490\_replaced([11158012](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_KlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) regarding UL-RTOA measurements and UL SRS-RSRP received from L1 layer[End CB007880-C][End CB007880-C-UPD001]

#### 3.21.2.6.0-3 UL Mitigation for remote interference Enhance power configuration for random access (ID: 11163434)

**3.21.2.6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11163438`)

UL Mitigation for remote interference
In case of remote interference appearance and mitigation action is activated  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

1. 5G-L2-PS shall indicate RI state to Cplane to trigger corresponding RI mitigation.

When RI disappears or mitigation is deactivated, L2-PS shall indicate RI state to Cplane to cancel existing mitigations  (see 5G\_CP\_OTH\_8428\_replaced([11605165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y4JzWfwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

1. 5G-L2-PS shall set TPC command in all UL grants of MSG2(RAR) with value of nrRimRarTpcCommand, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9270\_replaced([11152728](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksh3kfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR660863] When nrRimRarTpcCommand is re-configured, 5G-L2-PS shall apply its new value immediately for mitigation configuration. [End PR660863]

When remote interference is over, 5G-L2-PS shall cancel above mitigation.

#### 3.21.2.6.0-4 UL Mitigation for remote interference trigger of RIM UL mitigation extension (ID: 11163444)

**3.21.2.6.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11163456`)

UL Mitigation for remote interference
In case of MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimMitigationExtend = "true", if gNB-DU confirmed remote interference appearance (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342\_replaced([11161667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , gNB-DU shall trigger RIM UL mitigation extension as below:

- UL Link Adaptation for RIM UL mitigation extension (seen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27204\_replaced([11130149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_efvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- Excluding UE from UL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set in 1st UL slot due to RIM UL mitigation extension (seen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27198\_replaced([11195190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv6iwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB012535-AA-UPD001] - excluding MSG3 initial transmissions  (seen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22029\_replaced([11177883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuyhafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and re-transmissions (seen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27198\_replaced([11195190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv6iwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from the 1st UL slot of each TDD pattern due to RIM UL mitigation extension. [END CB012535-AA-UPD001]

[CB012535-BA]- If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimStopUlClPc = “true”, gNB-DU force the final value TPC as 0dB (seen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2642\_replaced([11119253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).[End CB012535-BA]

[04305757]- excluding initial transmissions and re-transmissions of UL grant for contention resolution (seen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27198\_replaced([11195190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv6iwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  from the 1st UL slot of each TDD pattern due to RIM UL mitigation extension.[END 04305757]

If above condistions are not fully satisfied, gNB-DU shall stop RIM UL mitigation extension.

---

#### 3.21.2.7 Enter/Exit DL mitigation

##### 3.21.2.7.0-1 Enter/Exit DL mitigation Determine DL mitigation on RIM-RS detection (ID: 11163466)

**3.21.2.7.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11163490`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
[Before CB012719-A] 5G-L2-PS shall trigger DL mitigation (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26037\_replaced([11160995](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktRedvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) immediately for RIM RS detection according to following conditions [CB012719-A] L2PS shall consider the result of this evaluation as true, when all of the following conditions are met: [End CB012719-A]

If NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "0:disabled" and NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim = 3 (framework-0) or “4:framework-1” and (/NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is false)

>> AND If NRRIM\_PROFILE-nrRimMitigationScheme = { 2-DL mitigation or 3-UL and DL mitigation}

>> AND keeping in RI state2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

>> AND if RI state 2b is true due to RIM RS is detected (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200\_replaced([11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

>> AND the number of detected RIM-RS type 1 setIDs in the setID list is equal to or greater than /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numDetectedSetIdForMitigation

> > [Before CB012719-A][CB013350-A] AND 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29689\_replaced([11161107](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘Evaluation of conditional DL muting’ results with ‘DL muting’. [End CB013350-A][End CB012719-A]

[Before CB012719-A]

if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true, dynamic adjustment of K2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PDCCH muting on special slot BIx, y (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26037\_replaced([11160995](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktRedvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) take effect from the next PDCCH slot pattern (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4001\_replaced([11169142](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

gNB-DU shall keep DL mitigation running(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26037\_replaced([11160995](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktRedvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) until DL mitigation cancel conditions are met (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25970\_replaced([11163548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

gNB-DU shall check/determine if PDCCH and PDSCH on special slot and its preceding DL slot is muted (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26037\_replaced([11160995](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktRedvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when starting DL mitigation for RS detection trigger case. Depending on the result of this check, a fault shall be reported, see Note1.

Note1: the fault is reported by L3, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6239\_replaced([11230036](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyri7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for fault specification guidelines.

[End CB012719-A]

---

##### 3.21.2.7.0-2 Enter/Exit DL mitigation Manually triggered DL mitigation (ID: 11163496)

**3.21.2.7.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11163508`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
If [CB013350-A] all of the following conditions are met: [End CB013350-A]

* NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-actNrRim is not 0 and
* NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is NOT "0:disabled" and
* [Before CB012719-A][CB013350-A] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29689\_replaced([11161107](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSFivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ‘Evaluation of conditional DL muting’ results with ‘DL muting’ [End CB013350-A][End CB012719-A],

[Before CB012719-A] then gNB-DU shall trigger DL mitigation. [CB012719-A] then L2PS shall consider the result of this evaluation as true. [End CB012719-A]

[Before CB012719-A]

if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true, dynamic adjustment of K2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PDCCH muting on special slot BIx, y (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26035\_replaced([11160978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktRec_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is calculated during the generation of the next PDCCH slot pattern (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4001\_replaced([11169142](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_5861\_replaced([11362969](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc_m4vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after PDCCH DL mitigation status change.

gNB-DU shall keep DL mitigation running (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26035\_replaced([11160978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktRec_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) until DL mitigation cancel conditions are met (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25970\_replaced([11163548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktaBV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

gNB shall cancel the active fault-7535 regarding RIM DL mitigation. If timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi (defined by /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDlMitigationDurationWoRi) is not expired, timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi shall be stopped.

gNB shall display RIM DL mitigation information in fault-7527 only when NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is equal to "0:disabled", see Note1.

Note1: the content tagged with PR750314 shall be implemented for 24R2 only due to CB009823-B is LLF subfeature, and it is not valid for 24R3 because RIM DL mitigation will be reported with fault-7535 from 24R3.

[End CB012719-A]

---

##### 3.21.2.7.0-3 Enter/Exit DL mitigation Determine DL mitigation based on RI detection (ID: 11163514)

**3.21.2.7.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11163523`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
[CB012719-A] L2PS shall consider the result of this evaluation as true, when all of the following conditions are met: [End CB012719-A]

If NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "0:disabled" and NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is (1 or 2)

- If (/NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is true)

o Start counting the number of events that RI is detected (RI state 2a is true due to RI is detected (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342))

o If [CB013350-A] all of the following conditions are met: [End CB013350-A]

-- RI state 2a is true due to RI is detected (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342) and

-- the number of consecutive RI monitor windows with RI detected is equal to or greater than /NTBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numWinRiDetectForDlMitigation and

-- [Before CB012719-A][CB013350-A] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29689 ‘Evaluation of conditional DL muting’ results with ‘DL muting’ [End CB013350-A]

Then gNB-DU shall trigger DL mitigation as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26041. [End CB012719-A]

[Before CB012719-A]

if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true, dynamic adjustment of K2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484) and PDCCH muting on special slot BIx, y (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26041) is calculated during the generation of the next PDCCH slot pattern (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4001, 5G\_UP\_5861\_replaced([11362969](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc_m4vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after PDCCH DL mitigation status change.

gNB-DU shall keep DL mitigation running(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26041) until DL mitigation cancel conditions are met (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25970).

gNB shall check/determine if PDCCH and PDSCH on special slot and its preceding DL slot is muted (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26041) when starting DL mitigation. Depending on the result of this check, a fault shall be reported, see Note1.

Note1: the fault is reported by L3, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6239 for fault specification guidelines.

[End CB012719-A]

---

##### 3.21.2.7.0-4 Enter/Exit DL mitigation Determine DL mitigation based on mixed RIM-RS and RI detection (ID: 11163530)

**3.21.2.7.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11163541`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
[CB012719-A]  L2PS shall consider the result of this evaluation as true, when all of the following conditions are met: [End CB012719-A]

If NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "0:disabled" and (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is (3 or 4)) AND (/NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is true) AND (/NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRimMitigationScheme is { 2-DL mitigation or 3-UL and DL mitigation })),

- Start counting the number of events that RI is detected (RI state 2a is true due to RI is detected (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342))

- if [CB013350-A] one of the following conditions is met: [End CB013350-A]

-- RI state 2a is true due to RI is detected and (the number of consecutive RI monitor windows with RI detected is equal to greater than /NTBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numWinRiDetectForDlMitigation) [Before CB012719-A] [CB013350-A] and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29689 ‘Evaluation of conditional DL muting’ results with ‘DL muting’ [End CB013350-A] [End CB012719-A] or

-- RI state 2b is true due to RIM RS is detected (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200)  and the number of detected RIM-RS type 1 setIDs in the setID list is equal to or greater than /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numWinRiDetectForDlMitigation [Before CB012719-A] [CB013350-A] and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29689 ‘Evaluation of conditional DL muting’ results with ‘DL muting’ [End CB013350-A] [End CB012719-A] ,

then gNB-DU shall trigger DL mitigation as specified in [Before CB012719-A]5G\_UP\_ALG\_26039[CB012719-A]5G\_UP\_ALG\_29900[End CB012719-A].

[Before CB012719-A]

if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMutingOnSpecialSlot is true, dynamic adjustment of K2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484) and PDCCH muting on special slot BIx, y (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26039) is calculated during the generation of the next PDCCH slot pattern (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4001,5G\_UP\_5861\_replaced([11362969](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc_m4vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after PDCCH DL mitigation status change.

gNB-DU shall keep DL mitigation running(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26039)  until DL mitigation cancel conditions are met (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25970).

gNB shall check/determine if PDCCH and PDSCH on special slot and its preceding DL slot is muted (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26039) when starting DL mitigation. Depending on the result of this check, a fault shall be reported, see Note1.

Note1: the fault is reported by L3, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6239 for fault specification guidelines.

[End CB012719-A]

##### 3.21.2.7.0-5 Enter/Exit DL mitigation Conditions for manually triggered DL mitigation with range adjustment (ID: 13432608)

**3.21.2.7.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13432613`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
Determine manually triggered with RIM-RS based DL mitigation

---

**3.21.2.7.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13432614`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
L2PS shall consider the result of this evaluation as true, when all of the following conditions are met:

* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimManualMitigationRangeAdj is set to true.
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is greater than 0.
* NRCELL.actNRRim is 3 (framework-0) or 4 (framework-1).
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is set to false.
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRimMitigationScheme is 2 (DL mitigation) or 3 (UL and DL mitigation).
* RI state 2b is active due to the detection of RIM-RS (see [11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* The number of detected RIM-RS type 1 setIDs in the setID list is equal to or greater than NRRIM\_PROFILE.numDetectedSetIdForMitigation.

Otherwise, L2PS shall consider the result of the evaluation as false.

---

**3.21.2.7.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13432617`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
Determine manually triggered with RI based DL mitigation

---

**3.21.2.7.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13432618`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
L2PS shall consider the result of this evaluation as true, when all of the following conditions are met:

* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimManualMitigationRangeAdj is set to true.
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is greater than 0.
* NRCELL.actNRRim is 1 (RI detection only) or 2 (RI detection and mitigation).
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is true.
* RI state 2a is active due to RI is detected.
* The number of consecutive RI monitor windows with RI detected is equal to or greater than NRRIM\_PROFILE.numWinRiDetectForDlMitigation.

Otherwise, L2PS shall consider the result of the evaluation as false.

---

**3.21.2.7.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13432621`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
Determine manually triggered with mixed RIM-RS & RI based DL mitigation

---

**3.21.2.7.0-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13432622`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
L2PS shall consider the result of this evaluation as true, when all of the following conditions are met:

* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimManualMitigationRangeAdj is set to true.
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is greater than 0.
* NRCELL.actNRRim is 3 (framework-0) or 4 (framework-1).
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is set to true.
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.nrRimMitigationScheme is 2 (DL mitigation) or 3 (UL and DL mitigation).
* One of the following conditions is met:
* RI state 2a is active due to RI is detected AND the number of consecutive RI monitor windows with RI detected is equal to greater than NRRIM\_PROFILE.numWinRiDetectForDlMitigation.
* RI state 2b is active due to RIM RS is detected (see [11163032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYMKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) AND the number of detected RIM-RS type 1 setIDs in the setID list is equal to or greater than NRRIM\_PROFILE.numDetectedSetIdForMitigation.

Otherwise, L2PS shall consider the result of the evaluation as false.

---

##### 3.21.2.7.0-6 Enter/Exit DL mitigation Cancel DL mitigation (ID: 11163548)

**3.21.2.7.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `13485524`)

Enter/Exit DL mitigation
13485524:
Enter/Exit DL mitigation
Note: RIM DL mitigation shall be considered as RIM DL muting or RIM DL power reduction
If *NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is 0, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
Else if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "0:disabled" and if [Before 05613403-26R3] NRBTS/NRCELL-tmpParam7[05613403-26R3] NRRIM\_PROFILE.RiPilotMode [End 05613403] is NOT "3:postDetection",*
- If /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is false,

> If *NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is NOT set 3 (framework-0)  and NOT “4:framework-1, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.*
> else if RI state2b exits due to RIM-RS disappears (see [5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_13200)),  gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
> else if the number of**detected RIM-RS type 1 setIDs in the setID list is less than***/NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numDetectedSetIdForMitigation**, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.****\***else if RI state2 is false (see [5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_9324)), gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
> else if*NRRIM\_PROFILE-nrRimMitigationScheme\*is not set as**{ 2-DL mitigation or 3-UL and DL mitigation*}, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.****\*
>  else if [5G\_UP\_ALG\_29689](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_29689) ‘Evaluation of conditional DL muting’ results with value other than ‘DL muting’, gNB-DU shall stop RIM DL muting.
> - else if /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is true,
> If NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is (1 or 2)*\*and /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDlMitigationDurationWoRi = 0 and RI state 2a is false, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.**
> else if NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is (1 or 2)  and /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDlMitigationDurationWoRi > 0 and RI state 2a becomes false when DL mitigation is ongoing, timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi (defined by /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDlMitigationDurationWoRi) shall start. When timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi expires, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation from next RIM session if RI state 2a keeps being false.
> else if (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is (3 or 4)) AND (RI state 2 is false), gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
> else if (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is 3) AND (RI state 2b is false) AND (RI state 2a becomes false when DL mitigation is ongoing),
>
> > if /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDlMitigationDurationWoRi is equal to 0, stop DL mitigation.
> > else timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi (defined by /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/minDlMitigationDurationWoRi) shall start.
> >
> > > If timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi expires, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation When timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi expires, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation from next RIM session if RI state 2a keeps being false.
> > > else if NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is NOT set 3 (framework-0), gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
> > > else if NRRIM\_PROFILE-nrRimMitigationScheme is not set as { 2-DL mitigation or 3-UL and DL mitigation }, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
> > > else if (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is 3) AND (RI state 2b is true) AND (RI state 2a becomes false when DL mitigation is ongoing),
> > > if *maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi*defined by */NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi is greater than 0, timer*maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi*shall start,****\*
> > > if timer*maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi\*expires, stop DL mitigation from next RIM session if RI state 2a keeps being false.**
> > > *>>>*else if RI stat2b becomes false, stop DL mitigation.**else if NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is NOT set 3 (framework-0), gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.

Timer *maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi shall still run.****\*******\***else if*NRRIM\_PROFILE-nrRimMitigationScheme\*is not set as**{ 2-DL mitigation or 3-UL and DL mitigation*}, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation. > > > else if the number of**detected RIM-RS type**1**setIDs in the setID list is less than***/NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numDetectedSetIdForMitigation**,**gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation. Timer*maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi shall still run.***\*******\****
> > > else if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-nrRimMitigationScheme*is not set as**{ 2-DL mitigation or 3-UL and DL mitigation*}, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation. Timer \*maxRsDetectDurationWithoutRi shall still run.******else if NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is NOT set 4 (framework-0), gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
> > > else
> > > if NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is NOT set 4 (framework-1), gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
> > > else if RI state2b is false (see [5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_9324)), gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
> > > else if the number of*\*detected RIM-RS type**1**setIDs in the setID list is less than***/NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numDetectedSetIdForMitigation**,**gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.****\*******\**
> > > else if *NRRIM\_PROFILE-nrRimMitigationScheme*is not set as**{ 2-DL mitigation or 3-UL and DL mitigation*}, gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.****\*
> > >  else if [5G\_UP\_ALG\_29689](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_29689) ‘Evaluation of conditional DL muting’ results with value other than ‘DL muting’, gNB-DU shall stop RIM DL muting.
> > > else if [5G\_UP\_ALG\_29689](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_29689) ‘Evaluation of conditional DL muting’ results with value other than ‘DL muting’, gNB-DU shall stop RIM DL muting.
> > > Else if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimDlMitigationManualTrigger is "0:disabled" and if NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRiPilotDlMute =true and [Before 05613403-26R3] NRBTS/NRCELL-tmpParam7 [05613403-26R3] NRRIM\_PROFILE.RiPilotMode [End 05613403-26R3] = 3:postDetection,
> > > - If /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is false,
> > > if RI state2b exits due to RIM-RS disappears (see [5G\_UP\_ALG\_13200](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_13200)), 
> > > Or if the number of detected RIM-RS type 1 setIDs in the setID list is less than /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numDetectedSetIdForMitigation,
> > > Or if RI state2 is false (see [5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_9324)),
> > > - else If /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRiDetectTriggerDlMitigation is true AND
> > >  if NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is (1 or 2)  and RI state 2a becomes false and DL mitigation is ongoing
> > > or if (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is (3 or 4)) AND (RI state 2 is false),
> > > or if (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is 3) AND (RI state 2b is false) AND (RI state 2a becomes false when DL mitigation is ongoing) AND
> > > or if (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is 3) AND (RI state 2b is true) AND (RI state 2a becomes false when DL mitigation is ongoing) AND
> > > if RI stat2b becomes false
> > > or if the number of detected RIM-RS type 1 setIDs in the setID list is less than /NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/numDetectedSetIdForMitigation,
> > > or if (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is 4) AND (RI state 2b is false) AND (RI state 2c is true) AND (RI state 2a becomes false when DL mitigation is ongoing) AND
> > > or if (NRBTS/NRCell-actNRRim is 4) AND (RI state 2b is true) AND (RI state 2a becomes false when DL mitigation is ongoing) AND
> > > if (RI state 2b becomes false)
> > > - in above any case, gNB-DU shall start Ri Pilot processing, then
> > > If RI disappearance is confirmed in ongoing Ri pilot processing in [12584537: Determine DL muting in RI pilot period](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_kFnVIDVEEfCKaNlcHOQWmg)) ,  gNB-DU shall stop DL mitigation.
> > > If DL mitigation is stopped,
> > > - gNB-DU shall take recovery actions to stop muting PDSCH in special slot BIx y or the DL slot (DL14 ) before special slot (see [5G\_UP\_ALG\_12626](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_12626)).*\*-**if timer minDlMitigationDurationWoRi is not expired, it shall be stopped. 
> > > 5G-L2-PS shall notify CP-RT when DL mitigation is stopped.***\*
> > >

### 3.21.2.8 Post processing after RIM-RS detection

#### 3.21.2.8.0-1 Post processing after RIM-RS detection Determination of Asymmetric indication (ID: 11163589)

**3.21.2.8.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11163596`)

Post processing after RIM-RS detection
11163596:
Post processing after RIM-RS detection
If NRBTS/NRCELL-actNrRim is configured to 4-“framework-1”, and if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-actRimAsymmetricIndication = "true", gNB-DU shall determine if the cell is in  "Asymmetric" status or not.

gNB-DU shall determine "Asymmetric" or "NotAsymmetric" status by checking (AsymmetricChecking) RI detected status (2a, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342) at the end of each repetition transmission window, [image-0][image\_desc]The image is too blurry to provide a detailed description or extract any text or tables.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11304.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] =R1-1,  [Before PR787630] of own RS type1 transmission [PR787630] which is calculated for own RS type1 transmission occasion, no matter if own RS type1 transmission is triggered or not [End PR787630] (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12684) , as below:

* if RI is detected (2a=true, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342) at any AsymmetricChecking,

> if no existing counting for RS period duration, gNB-DU shall start counting the number of experienced RS transmission periods (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12626) initiated from 1.

> else, gNB-DU shall keep counting the number of experienced RS transmission periods by incrementing 1.

* else  if RI is NOT detected (2a=false) at any AsymmetricChecking

> gNB-DU shall end existing count of the number of experienced RS transmission periods (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12626) .
>
> gNB-DU shall indicate the cell as "NotAsymmetric" upon there is state change;

-if the experienced number of RS transmission period is equal or larger than the threshold given by NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-rimAsymmetricDetectionWindow , after that gNB-DU shall additionally check RI detected status at the 2nd NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE-NRRIMonitorWindow (2a, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342),

> if RI is checked as RI detected (2a=true) , the cell shall be indicated as "Asymmetric" upon there is state change.

> else RI is checked as NOT detected, the cell shall be indicated as "NotAsymmetric" upon there is state change, end existing count;

---

#### 3.21.2.8.0-2 Post processing after RIM-RS detection Asymmetric state report via fault or CM parameter (ID: 11163602)

**3.21.2.8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11163608`)

Post processing after RIM-RS detection
If NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/asymmetricStateReport is configured to 0, gNB-DU shall disable Asymmetric state reporting via fault-7532 or CM parameter NRCELL/[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO[End CB014133-A-UPD002]/asymmetricState.

Else if NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/asymmetricStateReport is configured to 1[CB014133-A-UPD002] and NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimAsymmetricIndication is true[End CB014133-A-UPD002], gNB-DU shall support to report Asymmetric state via CM parameter NRCELL/[Before CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIM\_INFO[CB014133-A-UPD002]NRRIMINFO[End CB014133-A-UPD002]/asymmetricState periodically, the reporting interval is equal to [Before CB014133-A-UPD002]rdRiUpdateInterval(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32375) \* [End CB014133-A-UPD002]NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow.

Else if NRBTS/actRimCmFmReport/asymmetricStateReport is configured to 2[CB014133-A-UPD002] and NRRIM\_PROFILE/actRimAsymmetricIndication is true[End CB014133-A-UPD002], gNB-DU shall support to report Asymmetric state via fault-7532 periodically, the reporting interval is equal to [Before CB014133-A-UPD002]rdRiUpdateInterval \* [End CB014133-A-UPD002]NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRiMonitorWindow.

---

#### 3.21.2.8.0-3 Post processing after RIM-RS detection Determination of Enough or NotEnough mitigation status (ID: 11163613)

**3.21.2.8.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11163621`)

Post processing after RIM-RS detection
11163621:
Post processing after RIM-RS detection
If NRBTS/NRCELL-actNrRim is configured to 4-“framework-1”, and if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE- actRsEnoughIndiation= "true", gNB-DU shall determine if the cell experience "Enough" or "NotEnough" mitigation status.

During RI state2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324), after gNB-DU start its own RS type1 transmission (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12735),  at the beginning of each repetition transmission window, [image-0][image\_desc]The image is too blurry to provide a detailed description or extract any text or tables.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11308.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] =0, of own RS type1 transmission (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12684), gNB-DU shall determine the "Enough" or "NotEnough" mitigation status for the cell by checking the RI detected status (RI 2a, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9342) as below cases:

 The cell shall be determined “NotEnough” as default status

 When RI became not detected (2a=false), the cell shall be determined and indicated as "Enough"

 When RI became detected (2a=true), the cell shall be determined and indicated as "NotEnough"

gNB-DU shall keep current indication until next determination of  "Enough" or "NotEnough".

---

#### 3.21.2.9 Interworking between periodic/aperiodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting on special slot

##### 3.21.2.9.0-1 Interworking between periodic/aperiodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting on special slot Interworking between periodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting (ID: 11163631)

**3.21.2.9.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11163637`)

Interworking between periodic/aperiodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting on special slot
When rrmK2min(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484) is equal to 2, gNB-DU shall support to schedule periodic SRS as below,

* if PDCCH on special slot is muted (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26032) and periodic SRS is not disabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13520),

> If slot N+3 is a special slot, gNB-DU shall support to schedule periodic SRS reception on slot N+3 from slot N.

---

##### 3.21.2.9.0-2 Interworking between periodic/aperiodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting on special slot Interworking between aperiodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting on special slot only (ID: 11163642)

**3.21.2.9.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13246469`)

Interworking between periodic/aperiodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting on special slot
When rrmK2min (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484) is equal to 2 [CB013330-D] AND (PDCCH muting on special slot is ongoing) AND (PDCCH is not muted on DL slot),[End CB013330-D]

* if (NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDynamic[CB013330-D-UPD001]Srs[End CB013330-D-UPD001]SlotOffsetEnabled is equal to 0) and (PDCCH is muted on special slot),

-- if MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.tddFrameStructureType = tdLte, gNB-DU shall skip aperiodic SRS scheduling.

-- if  (MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.tddFrameStructureType = semiStatic and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.ulDlDataSlotRatio = 3/7),

> if (slot N is a DL slot) and (slot N+1 is a special slot) and (slot N+3 is an UL slot), gNB-DU shall skip aperiodic SRS scheduling on slot N+2 and slot N+3.

* if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDynamicSrsSlotOffsetEnabled is [Before CB013330-D-UPD001]equal to 1[CB013330-D-UPD001]greater than 0[End CB013330-D-UPD001],

-- gNB-DU shall indicate srsSlotOffset=3 to UE when PDCCH on special slot is muted.

-- when the trigger condition of aperiodic SRS request is met (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5057),

> If (PDCCH on special slot is muted) and (MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.tddFrameStructureType = tdLte) and (UE's srsSlotOffset is 3),

> > if (slot N is a DL slot) and (slot N+2 is a special slot), gNB-DU shall support to schedule aperiodic SRS on slot N+3 from slot N.
> >
> > if (slot N is a DL slot) and (slot N+1 is a special slot), gNB-DU shall support to schedule aperiodic SRS on slot N+3 from slot N.
>
> If (PDCCH on special slot is muted) and (MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.tddFrameStructureType = semiStatic and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.ulDlDataSlotRatio = 3/7),
>
> > if UE's srsSlotOffset is 3,
> >
> > > **if (slot N is a DL slot) and (slot N+2 is a special slot) and (slot N+4 is an UL slot), gNB-DU shall support to schedule aperiodic SRS on slot N+3 from slot N.**
> >
> > if (slot N is a DL slot) and (slot N+1 is a special slot) and (slot N+3 is an UL slot), gNB-DU shall support to schedule aperiodic SRS on slot N+3 from slot N.
> >
> > if UE's srsSlotOffset is 2,
> >
> > > if (slot N is a DL slot) and (slot N+1 is a special slot) and (slot N+2 is an UL slot ) and (slot N+3 is a DL slot), gNB-DU shall support to schedule aperiodic SRS on slot N+2 from slot N.
>
> if (PDCCH on special slot is not muted) and (UE's srsSlotOffset is 3), apSRS shall be skipped.

---

##### 3.21.2.9.0-3 Interworking between periodic/aperiodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting on special slot Interworking between aperiodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting on special slot and DL slot (ID: 13248520)

**3.21.2.9.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13248521`)

Interworking between periodic/aperiodic SRS scheduling and PDCCH muting on special slot
If PDCCH muting on special slot and DL slot is ongoing,

[CB013330-D-UPD001]- If UE's srsSlotOffset is 2, skip apSRS scheduling.[End CB013330-D-UPD001]

* If rrmK2min is 2 [CB013330-D-UPD001]and NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDynamicSrsSlotOffsetEnabled is not equal to 0[End CB013330-D-UPD001], gNB-DU shall allocate srsSlotOffset=3 to UE.
* If NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDynamic[CB013330-D-UPD001]Srs[End CB013330-D-UPD001]SlotOffsetEnabled is [Before CB013330-D-UPD001]not[End CB013330-D-UPD001] equal to 0, skip apSRS scheduling
* If NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDynamic[CB013330-D-UPD001]Srs[End CB013330-D-UPD001]SlotOffsetEnabled is equal to 1,

> if (NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.tddFrameStructureType = semiStatic and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.ulDlDataSlotRatio = 1/4) AND (UEs' srsSlotOffset is 3) AND (slot N+[Before CB013330-D-UPD001]1[CB013330-D-UPD001]2[End CB013330-D-UPD001] is a special slot) AND (slot N+3 is an UL slot),
>
> > schedule apSRS on slot N+3 from slot N
>
> else, skip apSRS scheduling

* If NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rimDynamic[CB013330-D-UPD001]Srs[End CB013330-D-UPD001]SlotOffsetEnabled is equal to 2,

> if (NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.tddFrameStructureType = semiStatic and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.ulDlDataSlotRatio = 1/4) AND (UEs' srsSlotOffset is 3) AND (slot N+[Before CB013330-D-UPD001]1[CB013330-D-UPD001]2[End CB013330-D-UPD001] is a special slot) AND (slot N+3 is an UL slot),
>
> > schedule apSRS on slot N+3 from slot N
>
> if  (NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.tddFrameStructureType = semiStatic and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.ulDlDataSlotRatio = [Before CB013330-D-UPD001]1/4[CB013330-D-UPD001]3/7[End CB013330-D-UPD001]) OR (NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.tddFrameStructureType = tdLte),
>
> > if (the arriving rate of apSRS requests in the last monitor window (which is fixed to 1 second) exceed rdAsrsArrivalRateThreshold) AND (UE's srsSlotOffset is 3),
> >
> > > suspend PDCCH muting on DL slot and switch current K2 to 3
> > >
> > > start timer timerNrRimTimeForAsrsScheduling defined by NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/nrRimTimeForAsrsScheduling
> > >
> > > perform apSRS scheduling as defined in [11163642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_GEGH8PvNEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) per demand until timerNrRimTimeForAsrsScheduling expires
> > >
> > > when timer timerNrRimTimeForAsrsScheduling expires, resume PDCCH muting on DL slot and switch current K2 accordingly.

[CB013330-D-UPD001]

Note1: the apSRS requests shall include the skipped apSRS scheduling due to PDCCH muting.

[End CB013330-D-UPD001]

---

#### 3.21.2.10 Interworking between aperiodic SRS scheduling and K2 change due to L2 CPU processing timing pattern switch and/or K2 mode switch

##### 3.21.2.10.0-1 Interworking between aperiodic SRS scheduling and K2 change due to L2 CPU processing timing pattern switch and/or K2 mode switch (ID: 11163658)

**3.21.2.10.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11163664`)

Interworking between aperiodic SRS scheduling and K2 change due to L2 CPU processing timing pattern switch and/or K2 mode switch
CPU processing timing pattern switch cases are defined in 5G\_UP\_13514\_replaced([11388917](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufMmXfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_13516\_replaced([11388957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufNNYPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_13523\_replaced([11389057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufNNY_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For a cell, if K2 for PUSCH is changed upon timing pattern switching and latest k2Rim is 3, then gNB-DU shall refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27958.

For a cell, if [CB013305-D] ( [End CB013305-D] K2 for PUSCH is changed upon timing pattern switching [CB013305-D] or K2 mode switching) [End CB013305-D] and latest k2Rim is not 3,

- [CB013305-D] if single K2 mode is being used (5G\_UP\_ALG\_30394), [End CB013305-D] denoted k2Pusch is the latest K2 for PUSCH. Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29578.

- [CB013305-D] if multiple K2 mode is being used, denoted k2Pusch is minimum K2 value in current K2 for PUSCH set (5G\_UP\_ALG\_30394 and 5G\_UP\_13617\_replaced([11348263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubTk3vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB013305-D]

- gNB-DU shall indicate srsSlotOffset= k2Pusch to new UE.

- When gNB-DU schedules a UL PDCCH in slot N for PUSCH of slot N+k2Pusch, if UE’s srsSlotOffset  is equal to k2Psuch, gNB-DU shall support to schedule aperiodic SRS on slot N+k2Pusch from slot N.

Reference:

* k2Rim: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484
* timing pattern switch: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29578.

---

## 3.21.3 Measurements

### 3.21.3.0-1 Measurements Number of used PRBs in RIM DL muted slots (ID: 11163675)

**3.21.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11163680`)

Measurements
When NRRIM\_PROFILE.highPrioRbTransInMutedSlots is set to true, then L2PS shall measure the accumulated number of PDSCH PRBs used in muted slots for UEs having radio bearers with priority equal to or higher than GBR. The accumulated number shall be increase by amount of scheduled PRBs in a DL grant of iniTx or reTx sent on PDCCH.

This information is used to update PRB\_USED\_PDSCH\_MUT\_HI\_PRI\_DATA counter value.

---

### 3.21.3.0-2 Measurements Number of used RIM DL muted slots (ID: 11163685)

**3.21.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11163690`)

Measurements
When NRRIM\_PROFILE.highPrioRbTransInMutedSlots is set to true, then L2PS shall measure the number of muted slots with PDSCH data scheduled for UEs having radio bearers with priority equal to or higher than GBR.

This information is used to update NUM\_MUT\_SLOT\_SCHD\_HI\_PRI\_DATA counter value.

---

### 3.21.3.0-3 Measurements RIM DL power reduction duration (ID: 11163696)

**3.21.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12632159`)

Measurements
When NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimPowerReduction is set to true, then L2PS shall measure total duration for which power reduction criteria are met. Counters shall be collected separately for special slot, downlink slot before special slot and second downlink slot before special slot. They shall be updated only when all of the following rules are fulfilled:

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29886 'Evaluation of DL mitigation' results with true
* NRRIM\_PROFILE.actRimPowerReduction is set to true
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29691 'Evaluation if cell load is above threshold' results with true
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29884 'RIM DL muting fallback timer' has not yet expired

This information is used to update DUR\_1ST\_DL\_PWR\_RED\_RIM\_MITG, DUR\_2ND\_DL\_PWR\_RED\_RIM\_MITG, DUR\_DL\_SPCL\_PWR\_RED\_RIM\_MITG, [CB014153-A] DUR\_3RD\_DL\_PWR\_RED\_RIM\_MITG [End CB014153-A] counters value.

---

### 3.21.3.0-4 Measurements Detected units for new RIM-RS detection (ID: 12698742)

**3.21.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12698743`)

Measurements
L2PS shall measure the number of L1 detected units for new RIM-RS detection. The measurement shall be executed for each slot where RIM-RS signal detection has been requested.

---

## 3.21.4 R&amp;D parameters

### 3.21.4.0-1 R&amp;D parameters rdRiMonitorAllSsb (ID: 11163711)

**3.21.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11163717`)

R&D parameters
Defines whether to enable monitoring RI on the first UL symbol with all SSB beam during each RI session

Value range: 0,...1

Default value: 1

Unit: NA

Online modifiable: Yes

Step Size: 1

Specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31912.

### 3.21.4.0-2 R&amp;D parameters rdRimSmoothAlpha (ID: 11163724)
